# FiguraMC

This wiki is under heavy construction.

To contribute to this wiki, see [Wanted Pages](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Special:WantedPages "Special:WantedPages")
, [Stubs](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Category:Stubs "Category:Stubs")
, and [Contributing](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/FiguraMC:Contributing "FiguraMC:Contributing")
.

[**Looking for the old wiki? Click here!**](https://figura-wiki.pages.dev/)

# Vectors and Matrices - FiguraMC

(Redirected from [Matrix2](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Matrix2&redirect=no "Matrix2")
)

This page is a [stub](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Stub "wikipedia:Wikipedia:Stub")
. You can help this wiki by [expanding it](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Vectors_and_Matrices&action=edit)

Not to be confused with [Vectors (Global)](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Vectors_(Global)&action=edit&redlink=1 "Vectors (Global) (page does not exist)")
, [Vector](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector "Vector")
, or [Matrices (Global)](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Matrices_(Global)&action=edit&redlink=1 "Matrices (Global) (page does not exist)")
.

Vectors and matrices at their core are **a set of numbers** that represent something (e.g. a Vector3 could represent a position in the world.)

Vectors are one-dimensional; for example, a [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3")
 holds 3 numbers. Vectors are most commonly used for representing the position and rotation of things.

Matrices are two-dimensional grids. All matrices are square, so a Matrix3 is a 3 by 3 grid of numbers. Matrices are most commonly used to represent transformations of vectors. For more in-depth information, see [the Wikipedia article on transformation matrices](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Transformation_matrix "wikipedia:Transformation matrix")
.

Vectors
-------

Many functions that take in a vector will also take in the same amount of numbers and internally convert it into a Vector.

Vectors come in 3 types: Vector2, Vector3, and Vector4. The number refers to the size of the vector (Vector4 has 4 numbers, etc.) You can create a vector by using the global method `vec` as shown:

*   vec(x [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
    , y [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
    , z [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
     | [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
    , w [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
     | [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
    )

This method will return a vector based on how many arguments you input.

Matrices
--------

Matrices are a set of vectors, which are normally used to change where models are, how they look, etc.

# Vectors and Matrices - FiguraMC

(Redirected from [Matrix3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Matrix3&redirect=no "Matrix3")
)

This page is a [stub](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Stub "wikipedia:Wikipedia:Stub")
. You can help this wiki by [expanding it](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Vectors_and_Matrices&action=edit)

Not to be confused with [Vectors (Global)](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Vectors_(Global)&action=edit&redlink=1 "Vectors (Global) (page does not exist)")
, [Vector](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector "Vector")
, or [Matrices (Global)](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Matrices_(Global)&action=edit&redlink=1 "Matrices (Global) (page does not exist)")
.

Vectors and matrices at their core are **a set of numbers** that represent something (e.g. a Vector3 could represent a position in the world.)

Vectors are one-dimensional; for example, a [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3")
 holds 3 numbers. Vectors are most commonly used for representing the position and rotation of things.

Matrices are two-dimensional grids. All matrices are square, so a Matrix3 is a 3 by 3 grid of numbers. Matrices are most commonly used to represent transformations of vectors. For more in-depth information, see [the Wikipedia article on transformation matrices](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Transformation_matrix "wikipedia:Transformation matrix")
.

Vectors
-------

Many functions that take in a vector will also take in the same amount of numbers and internally convert it into a Vector.

Vectors come in 3 types: Vector2, Vector3, and Vector4. The number refers to the size of the vector (Vector4 has 4 numbers, etc.) You can create a vector by using the global method `vec` as shown:

*   vec(x [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
    , y [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
    , z [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
     | [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
    , w [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
     | [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
    )

This method will return a vector based on how many arguments you input.

Matrices
--------

Matrices are a set of vectors, which are normally used to change where models are, how they look, etc.

# Vectors and Matrices - FiguraMC

(Redirected from [MatricesAPI](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=MatricesAPI&redirect=no "MatricesAPI")
)

This page is a [stub](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Stub "wikipedia:Wikipedia:Stub")
. You can help this wiki by [expanding it](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Vectors_and_Matrices&action=edit)

Not to be confused with [Vectors (Global)](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Vectors_(Global)&action=edit&redlink=1 "Vectors (Global) (page does not exist)")
, [Vector](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector "Vector")
, or [Matrices (Global)](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Matrices_(Global)&action=edit&redlink=1 "Matrices (Global) (page does not exist)")
.

Vectors and matrices at their core are **a set of numbers** that represent something (e.g. a Vector3 could represent a position in the world.)

Vectors are one-dimensional; for example, a [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3")
 holds 3 numbers. Vectors are most commonly used for representing the position and rotation of things.

Matrices are two-dimensional grids. All matrices are square, so a Matrix3 is a 3 by 3 grid of numbers. Matrices are most commonly used to represent transformations of vectors. For more in-depth information, see [the Wikipedia article on transformation matrices](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Transformation_matrix "wikipedia:Transformation matrix")
.

Vectors
-------

Many functions that take in a vector will also take in the same amount of numbers and internally convert it into a Vector.

Vectors come in 3 types: Vector2, Vector3, and Vector4. The number refers to the size of the vector (Vector4 has 4 numbers, etc.) You can create a vector by using the global method `vec` as shown:

*   vec(x [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
    , y [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
    , z [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
     | [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
    , w [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
     | [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
    )

This method will return a vector based on how many arguments you input.

Matrices
--------

Matrices are a set of vectors, which are normally used to change where models are, how they look, etc.

# FiguraMC:Contributing - FiguraMC

This page is a [stub](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Stub "wikipedia:Wikipedia:Stub")
. You can help this wiki by [expanding it](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=FiguraMC:Contributing&action=edit)

Contributing to the Mod
-----------------------

Please refer to [the GitHub repo](https://github.com/FiguraMC/Figura/blob/1.20/CONTRIBUTING.md)

Contributing to the Wiki
------------------------

### Information

When contributing to this wiki, there are a couple things you should remember:

*   Follow the [rules](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/FiguraMC:Rules "FiguraMC:Rules")
    
*   Follow the [style guide](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/FiguraMC:Contributing/Style_Guide "FiguraMC:Contributing/Style Guide")
    

### Style Guide

_From [Style Guide](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/FiguraMC:Contributing/Style_Guide "FiguraMC:Contributing/Style Guide")
 ([edit](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=FiguraMC:Contributing/Style_Guide&action=edit)
)_

This page is a [stub](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Stub "wikipedia:Wikipedia:Stub")
. You can help this wiki by [expanding it](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=FiguraMC:Contributing&action=edit)

General Guidelines
------------------

*   Avoid writing in the first/second person
    *   Only write in the second person in tutorials
    *   Avoid using [personal pronouns](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_personal_pronouns "wikipedia:English personal pronouns")
        
    *   See [Grammatical person](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Grammatical_person "wikipedia:Grammatical person")
        
*   Properly capitalize wikilinks where it makes sense

Types
-----

When creating a type page, please use the following layout:

_From [TypeExample](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/FiguraMC:Contributing/Style_Guide/TypeExample "FiguraMC:Contributing/Style Guide/TypeExample")
 ([edit](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=FiguraMC:Contributing/Style_Guide/TypeExample&action=edit)
)_

Page title
==========

(Don't add an additional level-1 heading for the page title.)

If necessary, use `{{[host only](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Template:Host_only "Template:Host only") }}`, `{{[Notice](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Template:Notice "Template:Notice") |...}}`, or `{{[Notice/Warning](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Template:Notice/Warning "Template:Notice/Warning") |...}}`. For example:

This API is only available on the host.

For more information, see [Pings](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Pings "Pings")
.

  
(Important information about the type...)

Methods
-------

| Method | Brief description |
| --- | --- |
| [methodName](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/FiguraMC:Contributing#methodName) | description |
| [secondCategoryMethod](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/FiguraMC:Contributing#secondCategoryMethod) | Returns the position of the ModelPart as a [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") |

Fields
------

| Field | Description | Type |
| --- | --- | --- |
| field | Brief description | [type](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Type "Type") |
| TICK | Runs every tick the player is rendered | [Event](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Event_(type) "Event (type)") |

-------

| --- | --- |

| x [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)<br>, y [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)<br>, z [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)<br>, name [string](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)<br> \| [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) | [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) |

| --- | --- |

Each method in the table should link to the section more in-depth explaining it.

### Rules

_From [FiguraMC:Rules](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/FiguraMC:Rules "FiguraMC:Rules")
 ([edit](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=FiguraMC:Rules&action=edit)
)_

*   Keep it PG
*   No hateful language
*   Mainspace (no-prefix) pages should be informative content about Figura, community libraries, or addons
*   Example code needs to be tested before publishing!

### (Temporary) Getting an Account

Until account creation is set up, contact one of the wiki admins.

. You can help this wiki by [expanding it](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=FiguraMetatables&action=edit)

figuraMetatables is a table containing the metatables for every type figura adds. Modifying this table will change the metatable on the respective type

# External links search - FiguraMC

Wildcards such as "\*.wikipedia.org" may be used.  
Supported protocols: bitcoin:, ftp://, ftps://, geo:, git://, gopher://, http://, https://, irc://, ircs://, magnet:, mailto:, matrix:, mms://, news:, nntp://, redis://, sftp://, sip:, sips:, sms:, ssh://, svn://, tel:, telnet://, urn:, worldwind://, xmpp: (defaults to http:// and https:// if no protocol is specified).

External links search

Search pattern:

Namespace:

all(Main)TalkUserUser talkFiguraMCFiguraMC talkFileFile talkMediaWikiMediaWiki talkTemplateTemplate talkHelpHelp talkCategoryCategory talkModuleModule talk

Search

Retrieved from "[https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Special:LinkSearch](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Special:LinkSearch)
"

# EventsAPI - FiguraMC

(Redirected from [Events](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events&redirect=no "Events")
)

Not to be confused with [Event](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Event "Event")
.

Events is a global which contains every [Event](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Event_(type) "Event (type)")
, which are fired when certain things happen. For example, if you want to count ticks, you can use the tick or world tick event.

local tick \= 0

\-- Register event
function events.TICK()
  tick \= tick + 1
end
\-- or
events.TICK:register(function()
  tick \= tick + 1
end)

Note that not everyone needs to count ticks

Methods
-------

| Method | Description |
| --- | --- |
| [getEvents](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Events#getEvents) | Returns a table of every event |

Fields
------

| Event | Description |
| --- | --- |
| [ENTITY\_INIT](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/ENTITY_INIT&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/ENTITY INIT (page does not exist)") | Runs when the player is loaded |
| [TICK](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/TICK&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/TICK (page does not exist)") | Runs every tick the player is rendered |
| [WORLD\_TICK](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/WORLD_TICK&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/WORLD TICK (page does not exist)") | Runs every tick the world is rendered |
| [RENDER](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/RENDER&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/RENDER (page does not exist)") | Runs every frame the player is rendered |
| [POST\_RENDER](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/POST_RENDER&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/POST RENDER (page does not exist)") | Runs every frame AFTER the player is rendered |
| [WORLD\_RENDER](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/WORLD_RENDER&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/WORLD RENDER (page does not exist)") | Runs every frame the world is rendered |
| [POST\_WORLD\_RENDER](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/POST_WORLD_RENDER&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/POST WORLD RENDER (page does not exist)") | Runs every frame AFTER the world is rendered |
| [SKULL\_RENDER](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/SKULL_RENDER&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/SKULL RENDER (page does not exist)") | Runs every frame for every skull when the skull is rendered. |
| [ARROW\_RENDER](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/ARROW_RENDER&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/ARROW RENDER (page does not exist)") | Runs every frame for every arrow when rendered. |
| [TRIDENT\_RENDER](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/TRIDENT_RENDER&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/TRIDENT RENDER (page does not exist)") | Runs every frame for every trident when rendered. |
| [ITEM\_RENDER](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/ITEM_RENDER&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/ITEM RENDER (page does not exist)") | Runs every frame for every item when rendered. |
| [CHAT\_SEND\_MESSAGE](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/CHAT_SEND_MESSAGE&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/CHAT SEND MESSAGE (page does not exist)") | Runs every time the player sends something in chat, including commands. Allows for changing the message |
| [CHAT\_RECEIVE\_MESSAGE](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/CHAT_RECEIVE_MESSAGE&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/CHAT RECEIVE MESSAGE (page does not exist)") | Runs every time the player receives something in chat. Allows for changing the message |
| [MOUSE\_SCROLL](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/MOUSE_SCROLL&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/MOUSE SCROLL (page does not exist)") | Runs every time the mouse is scrolled. Allows for cancelling the vanilla function |
| [MOUSE\_MOVE](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/MOUSE_MOVE&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/MOUSE MOVE (page does not exist)") | Runs every time the mouse is moved. Allows for cancelling the vanilla function |
| [MOUSE\_PRESS](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/MOUSE_PRESS&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/MOUSE PRESS (page does not exist)") | Runs every time the mouse is clicked. Allows for cancelling the vanilla function |
| [KEY\_PRESS](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/KEY_PRESS&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/KEY PRESS (page does not exist)") | Runs every time a key is pressed. Allows for cancelling the vanilla function |
| [CHAR\_TYPED](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/CHAR_TYPED&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/CHAR TYPED (page does not exist)") | Runs every time a character is typed. |
| [USE\_ITEM](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/USE_ITEM&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/USE ITEM (page does not exist)") | Runs every time an item is used by the player. |
| [ON\_PLAY\_SOUND](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/ON_PLAY_SOUND&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/ON PLAY SOUND (page does not exist)") | Runs every time a sound is played |
| [RESOURCE\_RELOAD](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/RESOURCE_RELOAD&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/RESOURCE RELOAD (page does not exist)") | Runs every time resources are reloaded |
| [TOTEM](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/TOTEM&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/TOTEM (page does not exist)") | Runs every time a totem of undying is activated |
| [DAMAGE](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/DAMAGE&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/DAMAGE (page does not exist)") | Runs whenever the player takes damage |

Methods
-------

#### getEvents

* * *

Returns a table of every event

\-- Example function to clear all events
function clearEvents()
  for \_, v in pairs(events:getEvents()) do
    v:clear()
  end
end

Retrieved from "[https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=EventsAPI&oldid=569](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=EventsAPI&oldid=569)
"

# Tracking categories - FiguraMC

This page lists tracking categories which are automatically populated by the MediaWiki software. Their names can be changed by altering the relevant system messages in the MediaWiki namespace.

| Tracking category | Message name | Category inclusion criteria |
| --- | --- | --- |
| [Pages with broken file links](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Category:Pages_with_broken_file_links&action=edit&redlink=1 "Category:Pages with broken file links (page does not exist)") | [broken-file-category](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/MediaWiki:Broken-file-category "MediaWiki:Broken-file-category") | The page contains a broken file link (a link to embed a file when the file does not exist). |
| [Pages using duplicate arguments in template calls](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Category:Pages_using_duplicate_arguments_in_template_calls&action=edit&redlink=1 "Category:Pages using duplicate arguments in template calls (page does not exist)") | [duplicate-args-category](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/MediaWiki:Duplicate-args-category "MediaWiki:Duplicate-args-category") | The page contains template calls that use duplicates of arguments, such as `{{foo\|bar=1\|bar=2}}` or `{{foo\|bar\|1=baz}}`. |
| [Pages where expansion depth is exceeded](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Category:Pages_where_expansion_depth_is_exceeded&action=edit&redlink=1 "Category:Pages where expansion depth is exceeded (page does not exist)") | [expansion-depth-exceeded-category](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/MediaWiki:Expansion-depth-exceeded-category "MediaWiki:Expansion-depth-exceeded-category") | The page exceeds the maximum expansion depth. |
| [Pages with too many expensive parser function calls](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Category:Pages_with_too_many_expensive_parser_function_calls&action=edit&redlink=1 "Category:Pages with too many expensive parser function calls (page does not exist)") | [expensive-parserfunction-category](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/MediaWiki:Expensive-parserfunction-category "MediaWiki:Expensive-parserfunction-category") | The page uses too many expensive parser functions (like `#ifexist`). See [Manual:$wgExpensiveParserFunctionLimit](https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Manual:$wgExpensiveParserFunctionLimit)<br>. |
| [Hidden categories](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Category:Hidden_categories&action=edit&redlink=1 "Category:Hidden categories (page does not exist)") | [hidden-category-category](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/MediaWiki:Hidden-category-category "MediaWiki:Hidden-category-category") | The category contains `__HIDDENCAT__` in its page content, which prevents it from showing up in the category links box on pages by default. |
| [Indexed pages](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Category:Indexed_pages&action=edit&redlink=1 "Category:Indexed pages (page does not exist)") | [index-category](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/MediaWiki:Index-category "MediaWiki:Index-category") | The page has a `__INDEX__` on it (and is in a namespace where that flag is allowed), and hence is indexed by robots where it normally wouldn't be. |
| [Pages where node count is exceeded](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Category:Pages_where_node_count_is_exceeded&action=edit&redlink=1 "Category:Pages where node count is exceeded (page does not exist)") | [node-count-exceeded-category](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/MediaWiki:Node-count-exceeded-category "MediaWiki:Node-count-exceeded-category") | The page exceeds the maximum node count. |
| [Noindexed pages](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Category:Noindexed_pages&action=edit&redlink=1 "Category:Noindexed pages (page does not exist)") | [noindex-category](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/MediaWiki:Noindex-category "MediaWiki:Noindex-category") | The page is not indexed by robots because it has the magic word `__NOINDEX__` on it and is in a namespace where that flag is allowed. |
| [Pages with non-numeric formatnum arguments](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Category:Pages_with_non-numeric_formatnum_arguments&action=edit&redlink=1 "Category:Pages with non-numeric formatnum arguments (page does not exist)") | [nonnumeric-formatnum](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/MediaWiki:Nonnumeric-formatnum "MediaWiki:Nonnumeric-formatnum") | The page contains a non-numeric argument to the formatnum parser function. |
| [Pages containing omitted template arguments](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Category:Pages_containing_omitted_template_arguments&action=edit&redlink=1 "Category:Pages containing omitted template arguments (page does not exist)") | [post-expand-template-argument-category](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/MediaWiki:Post-expand-template-argument-category "MediaWiki:Post-expand-template-argument-category") | The page is bigger than `$wgMaxArticleSize` after expanding a template argument (something in triple braces, like `{{{Foo}}}`). |
| [Pages where template include size is exceeded](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Category:Pages_where_template_include_size_is_exceeded&action=edit&redlink=1 "Category:Pages where template include size is exceeded (page does not exist)") | [post-expand-template-inclusion-category](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/MediaWiki:Post-expand-template-inclusion-category "MediaWiki:Post-expand-template-inclusion-category") | The page size is bigger than `$wgMaxArticleSize` after expanding all the templates, so some templates were not expanded. |
| [Pages with ignored display titles](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Category:Pages_with_ignored_display_titles&action=edit&redlink=1 "Category:Pages with ignored display titles (page does not exist)") | [restricted-displaytitle-ignored](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/MediaWiki:Restricted-displaytitle-ignored "MediaWiki:Restricted-displaytitle-ignored") | The page has an ignored `{{DISPLAYTITLE}}` because it is not equivalent to the page's actual title. |
| [Pages which use = as a template](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Category:Pages_which_use_%3D_as_a_template&action=edit&redlink=1 "Category:Pages which use = as a template (page does not exist)") | [template-equals-category](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/MediaWiki:Template-equals-category "MediaWiki:Template-equals-category") | The page contains `{{=}}` but on this wiki that does not expand to `=`. This usage is deprecated; a future MediaWiki version will implement `{{=}}` as a parser function. |
| [Pages with template loops](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Category:Pages_with_template_loops&action=edit&redlink=1 "Category:Pages with template loops (page does not exist)") | [template-loop-category](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/MediaWiki:Template-loop-category "MediaWiki:Template-loop-category") | The page contains a template loop, ie. a template which calls itself recursively. |
| [Pages where the unstrip depth limit is exceeded](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Category:Pages_where_the_unstrip_depth_limit_is_exceeded&action=edit&redlink=1 "Category:Pages where the unstrip depth limit is exceeded (page does not exist)") | [unstrip-depth-category](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/MediaWiki:Unstrip-depth-category "MediaWiki:Unstrip-depth-category") | The page exceeds the unstrip depth limit. |
| [Pages where the unstrip size limit is exceeded](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Category:Pages_where_the_unstrip_size_limit_is_exceeded&action=edit&redlink=1 "Category:Pages where the unstrip size limit is exceeded (page does not exist)") | [unstrip-size-category](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/MediaWiki:Unstrip-size-category "MediaWiki:Unstrip-size-category") | The page exceeds the unstrip size limit. |
| [Pages with reference errors](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Category:Pages_with_reference_errors&action=edit&redlink=1 "Category:Pages with reference errors (page does not exist)") | [cite-tracking-category-cite-error](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/MediaWiki:Cite-tracking-category-cite-error "MediaWiki:Cite-tracking-category-cite-error") | Pages in this category have errors in the usage of references tags. |
| Category is disabled | [discussiontools-comments-before-first-heading-category](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/MediaWiki:Discussiontools-comments-before-first-heading-category "MediaWiki:Discussiontools-comments-before-first-heading-category") | The discussion page contains comments in the lede section (before first heading). This may cause the lede or the comments to be displayed incorrectly, especially in the mobile version and in mobile apps. |

# ModelPart - FiguraMC

(Redirected from [Models](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Models&redirect=no "Models")
)

A ModelPart represents a Cube, Mesh, or Group from Blockbench.

Via scripting, ModelParts can be modified dynamically to achieve whatever visuals you need (limited to Minecraft's rendering engine)

Accessing ModelParts
--------------------

_From [:ModelPart Indexing](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/ModelPart_Indexing "ModelPart Indexing")
 ([edit](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=ModelPart_Indexing&action=edit)
)_

  
When Figura loads your avatar, all the model files in your avatar are organized into a tree. The starting point of this tree is called `models`. All of the parts of your model, including cubes, meshes, and groups from your Blockbench models, as well as folders in your avatar and the model files themselves are converted to ModelParts and part of this tree.

The name `models` does not refer to any specific model file in your avatar. Instead, model files are created as children of the `models` folder. **If your Blockbench model is inside a subfolder of your avatar**, that folder becomes a child of `models`, and the model file becomes a child of the subfolder.

![](https://wiki.figuramc.org/images/5/55/BBModel.png)`model.bbmodel`

![](https://wiki.figuramc.org/images/7/77/BBGroup.png)root

![](https://wiki.figuramc.org/images/7/77/BBGroup.png)Head

![](https://wiki.figuramc.org/images/1/1c/BBCube.png)Head

![](https://wiki.figuramc.org/images/1/1c/BBCube.png)HeadLayer

![](https://wiki.figuramc.org/images/7/77/BBGroup.png)RightArm

![](https://wiki.figuramc.org/images/1/1c/BBCube.png)RightArm

![](https://wiki.figuramc.org/images/1/1c/BBCube.png)RightArmLayer

![](https://wiki.figuramc.org/images/1/1c/BBCube.png)Cool Name

![](https://wiki.figuramc.org/images/7/77/BBGroup.png)Cool Group

![](https://wiki.figuramc.org/images/1/1c/BBCube.png)cube

To access a child part, _index_ the parent part with the name of the child part.

There are two ways to _index_ something in Lua. The first way is by using dots:

`models.model.root.Head`

This code sample first gets the `model` part (a file named `model.bbmodel`) and then the `Head` group inside it. The name of the cube, mesh, group, folder, or file needs to be within the quotes. To access deeper parts (for example, a `HeadLayer` cube within the `Head` group), add more dots and names:

`models.model.root.Head.HeadLayer`

The second way to index is longer, and uses square brackets and quotes (`[""]`) to separate the names. **This method is required if the name of a part contains characters that aren't letters, numbers, or underscores**; this includes _names with spaces_, like `Right Arm`.

When using brackets to index, place the name **between the quotes**, and **don't include a period before it**:

*   `models["model"]["root"]["Cool Name"]` ✓ Correct
    
*   `models.model.root["Cool Name"]` ✓ Correct - both brackets and dots can be mixed together!
    
*   `models.model.root.["Cool Name"]` ✗ Incorrect: **don't put a dot `.` before the bracket `[`.**\
    \
*   `models.model.root[Cool Name]` ✗ Incorrect: **name in brackets is missing a set of quotes**\
    \
\
To return to using dots for indexing after using brackets, place the dot after the closing bracket:\
\
*   `models.model.root["Cool Group"].cube` ✓ Correct\
    \
*   `models.model.root["Cool Group"]cube` ✗ Incorrect: **missing dot `.` after bracket**\
    \
\
### A note on model files in folders\
\
If your Blockbench model file is within a folder in your avatar, the _folder_ will become a part of the ModelPart tree. That means that if a model file named `player.bbmodel` is located in a folder named `models`, the model file has to be accessed with `models.models.player` (or `models["models"]["player"]`.)\
\
If you later want to use animations from a model, folders affect the indexing into the `animations` table too - but the system is a little different.\
\
Instead of indexing the folder and then the file, _combine each folder name and the file name with a period `.` and index with the combined name_, even if the names of the folders and files contain special characters. For example, to get the animations from the `model 2.bbmodel` file in the `main models` folder:\
\
![](https://wiki.figuramc.org/images/f/f1/FSFolderClosed.png)`main models`\
\
![](https://wiki.figuramc.org/images/5/55/BBModel.png)`model 2.bbmodel`\
\
animations\["main models.model 2"\]\
\
ParentTypes\
-----------\
\
In Figura, a [ParentType](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/ParentType "ParentType")\
 is applied to a ModelPart causing the ModelPart to behave in a predefined way. This behavior includes acting as a vanilla part like the Head or LeftLeg, moving the rendering of special parts like held items, armor, or parrots, and binding the ModelPart to the World instead of the Player.\
\
ParentTypes can either be applied in Blockbench itself or via script.\
\
### ParentTypes via BlockBench\
\
To define a ParentType in Blockbench, the name of a Group must begin with a case-sensitive ParentType.\
\
For example, the `Head` ParentType causes the ModelPart to move and rotate like the vanilla Head. If you name a Group the following, it will have this ParentType:\
\
*   Head\
*   HEAD\
*   Head2\
*   HeadPhones\
\
If you name a group the following, **it will not** have the `Head` ParentType:\
\
*   head => 'head' is not a valid ParentType. Capitalization matters!\
*   BigHead => Does not begin with ParentType\
*   HeAd => 'HeAd' is not a valid ParentType. Capitalization matters!\
\
Do note that some English words naturally start with a ParentType which can cause unintended behavior!\
\
For example, the word "Guitar". Seems innocent, right? Well, "Guitar" starts with "Gui", and "Gui" is an alias for the ParentType `Hud`, a ParentType that binds the ModelPart to the Heads Up Display where the hotbar and inventory reside. This causes the ModelPart to not be visible, as [`Hud` parts have special rules](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=ParentType/Hud&action=edit&redlink=1 "ParentType/Hud (page does not exist)")\
. Be careful!\
\
Note: ParentTypes are sometimes called Keywords by legacy Figura users\
\
### ParentTypes via Script\
\
Calling the `setParentType` on _any_ ModelPart will override it's ParentType.\
\
Simply [access](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Models#Accessing_ModelParts)\
 the ModelPart, then call `setParentType` on it, passing in the ParentType as a string.\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
head:setParentType("RightArm")\
\
To remove a ParentType from a ModelPart, call `setParentType` with the string `"None"`\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
head:setParentType("None")\
\
ModelParts **do not** remember their original ParentType! If you need a ModelPart's original ParentType, store it in a variable for later:\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
local headParentType \= head:getParentType()\
head:setParentType("None")\
\
ModelPart methods\
-----------------\
\
### ModelPart properties\
\
Read-only properties of a ModelPart\
\
#### getName\
\
* * *\
\
Returns the name of this ModelPart. ModelParts can have duplicate names.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getName()` | [string](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
print(head:getName()) \--> "Head"\
\
#### getType\
\
* * *\
\
Returns the original type of this ModelPart. Can be `Cube`, `Mesh`, or `Group`. BBModels and folders are considered Groups. Cubes with no texture data are also considered Groups, as with no texture data their face data is stripped.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getType()` | `"Cube" \| "Mesh" \| "Group"` |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
print(head:getType()) \--> "Group"\
\
### Editing ModelPart hierarchy\
\
Methods relating to getting other ModelParts and manipulating the ModelPart tree\
\
#### getParent\
\
* * *\
\
Returns the parent of this ModelPart, or `nil` if this is `models` or a loose ModelPart created via script.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getParent()` | ModelPart \| [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
print(head:getParent()) \--> ModelPart(root)\
\
#### getChildren\
\
* * *\
\
Returns an array containing all children of this ModelPart\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getChildren()` | ModelPart\[\] |\
\
local root \= models.model.root\
printTable(root:getChildren()) \--\[\[\
ModelPart(Head), \
ModelPart(Body), \
ModelPart(RightArm), \
ModelPart(LeftArm), \
ModelPart(RightLeg), \
ModelPart(LeftLeg),\
\]\]\--\
\
#### isChildOf\
\
* * *\
\
Recursively checks if this child is a decedent of the provided ModelPart.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `isChildOf(part ModelPart)` | [boolean](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) |\
\
local model \= models.model\
local head \= model.root.Head\
print(head:isChildOf(model)) \--> true\
\
#### copy\
\
* * *\
\
Copies the data of this ModelPart, assigning it a new name, then returning it. The new name has nothing to do with ParentTypes. The children of the copy are references to the original ModelPart's children. Extra work needs to be done to recursively copy it's children. The [addChild](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Models#ModelPart_addChild)\
 method can then be used to add the copy to the ModelPart tree.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `copy(newName [string](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | ModelPart |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
\
local headCopy \= head:copy("NewHead")\
print(headCopy) \--> ModelPart(NewHead)\
\
\-- The parentType is copied with the ModelPart\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
\
local headCopy \= head:copy("NewHead")\
print(headCopy:getParentType()) \--> "Head"\
\
headCopy:setParentType("None")\
print(headCopy:getParentType()) \--> "None"\
\
**@see** [setParentType](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Models#setParentType)\
,, [getParentType](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Models#getParentType)\
,\
\
\-- Extra work is needed to deep copy a ModelPart's children as well\
local function deepCopy(model)\
    local copy \= model:copy(model:getName())\
    for \_, child in pairs(copy:getChildren()) do\
        copy:removeChild(child):addChild(deepCopy(child))\
    end\
    return copy\
end\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
local headCube \= head.Head\
\
\-- headCopyA contains references to head's children because it is a shallow copy\
local headCopyA \= head:copy("NewHead")\
print(headCopyA.Head \== headCube) \--> true\
\
\-- headCopyB contains true copies of head's children as it was passed through a function that recursively copies children\
local headCopyB \= deepCopy(head)\
print(headCopyB.Head \== headCube) \--> false\
\
**@see** [getName](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Models#getName)\
,, [getChildren](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Models#getChildren)\
,, [addChild](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Models#addChild)\
,, [removeChild](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Models#removeChild)\
,\
\
#### addChild\
\
* * *\
\
Adds the provided ModelPart as one of this ModelPart's children. Beware of adding a parent of this ModelPart as a child! This method returns this ModelPart for method chaining.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `addChild(part ModelPart)` | self ModelPart |\
\
local root \= models.model.root\
local headCopy \= root.Head:copy("NewHead")\
root:addChild(headCopy)\
headCopy:setPos(10,0,0)\
\
**@see** [copy](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Models#copy)\
,, [setPos](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Models#setPos)\
,\
\
#### removeChild\
\
* * *\
\
Removes a child from this ModelPart. Takes in the child ModelPart itself. This method returns this ModelPart for method chaining.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `removeChild(partToRemove ModelPart)` | self ModelPart |\
\
local root \= models.model.root\
local head \= root.Head\
root:removeChild(head) \-- Bye bye Head!\
\
\-- Head is still valid and can be re-added later, so long as we keep a variable referencing it.\
print(head) \--> ModelPart(Head)\
\
#### remove\
\
* * *\
\
Removes this ModelPart from the parent's child list. Returns self\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `remove()` | self ModelPart |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
head:remove() \-- Bye bye Head!\
\
\-- Head is still valid and can be re-added, so long as we keep a variable referencing it.\
print(head) \--> ModelPart(Head)\
models.model.root.LeftLeg:addChild(head)\
\
**@see** [addChild](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Models#addChild)\
,\
\
### Manipulation\
\
Methods relating to manipulating the ModelPart within physical space\
\
#### setPos\
\
* * *\
\
Sets the offset of the the position of the ModelPart. Position translation applies on the local rotation axis.\
\
`nil` values are interpreted as 0.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `setPos(pos [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") )` | self ModelPart |\
| `setPos(x [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) , y [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) , z [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | self ModelPart |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
\
\-- Move 10 units on the local y axis\
head:setPos(0, 10, 0)\
\
#### getPos\
\
* * *\
\
Returns the value that was used for `setPos`. Always 0,0,0 when script begins.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getPos()` | [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
\
print(head:getPos()) \--> vec(0,0,0)\
head:setPos(0, 10, 0)\
print(head:getPos()) \--> vec(0,10,0)\
\
**@see** [setPos](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Models#setPos)\
,\
\
#### setRot\
\
* * *\
\
Sets the rotation of the ModelPart. Rotates the ModelPart around the PivotPoint.\
\
Angles are interpreted as degrees. `nil` values are interpreted as 0.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `setRot(rot [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") )` | self ModelPart |\
| `setRot(pitch [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) , yaw [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) , roll [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | self ModelPart |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
\
\-- Rotate 45 degrees on the x axis, causing the avatar to look down\
head:setRot(0, 45, 0)\
\
#### getRot\
\
* * *\
\
Returns the value that was used for `setRot`. Will be the Rotation values defined in BlockBench when script begins.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getRot()` | [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
\
print(head:getRot()) \--> vec(0,0,0) -- Most ModelParts will not have a rotation set in blockbench\
head:setRot(45, 0, 0)\
print(head:getRot()) \--> vec(45,0,0)\
\
**@see** [setRot](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Models#setRot)\
,\
\
#### setScale\
\
* * *\
\
Sets the scale of the ModelPart. Scales the ModelPart around the PivotPoint.\
\
`nil` values are interpreted as 1. If a number is provided for x and both y and z are not defined, x will be used for all 3 axis.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `setScale(scale [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") )` | self ModelPart |\
| `setScale(scaleAll [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | self ModelPart |\
| `setScale(x [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) , y [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) , z [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | self ModelPart |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
\-- Double the size of the head\
head:setScale(2)\
\-- Squishes and stretches the entire model\
models.model:setScale(1.5, 0.75, 1.5)\
\
#### getScale\
\
* * *\
\
Returns the value that was used for `setScale`. Always 1,1,1 when script begins.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getScale()` | [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
\
print(head:getScale()) \--> vec(1,1,1)\
head:setScale(2)\
print(head:getScale()) \--> vec(2,2,2)\
\
**@see** [setScale](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Models#setScale)\
,\
\
#### setPivot\
\
* * *\
\
Sets the pivot point of the ModelPart. _This overrides the pivot point defined in blockbench._ It is recommended to use [setOffsetPivot](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Models#setOffsetPivot)\
, instead.\
\
`nil` values are interpreted as 0.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `setPivot(pivot [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") )` | self ModelPart |\
| `setPivot(x [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) , y [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) , z [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | self ModelPart |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
\
\-- For a normal size humanoid model, the Head's pivot point is usually at 0,24,0\
\-- If we assume that the Head cube is an 8x8x8 cube,\
\-- then the head will rotate around the center of the cube instead of the neck\
head:setPivot(0, 28, 0)\
\
#### getPivot\
\
* * *\
\
Returns the Pivot Point defined in BlockBench, or the value set by `setPivot` if it was already overwritten.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getPivot()` | [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
\
\-- The Head group's pivot point for a humanoid model is usually at 0,24,0\
print(head:getPivot()) \--> vec(0,24,0)\
head:setPivot(0,0,0)\
\-- We have completely ruined the rendering of this ModelPart\
print(head:getPivot()) \--> vec(0,0,0)\
\
**@see** [setPivot](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Models#setPivot)\
,\
\
#### setOffsetRot\
\
* * *\
\
Sets a rotation value that will be added to the ModelPart's rotation.\
\
Angles are interpreted as degrees. `nil` values are interpreted as 0.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `setOffsetRot(rot [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") )` | self ModelPart |\
| `setOffsetRot(pitch [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) , yaw [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) , roll [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | self ModelPart |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
\
\-- ModelParts inherit their rotation from blockbench. The Head usually has a rotation of 0,0,0 for consistency with the vanilla model\
print(head:getRot()) \--> vec(0,0,0)\
\-- Set the offset to 45 degrees on the x axis, causing the avatar to look down\
head:setOffsetRot(0, 45, 0)\
\-- The original rotation is unchanged.\
print(head:getRot()) \--> vec(0,0,0)\
\
\-- setOffsetRot is not additive.\
head:setOffsetRot(0, 25, 0)\
print(head:getOffsetRot()) \--> vec(0,25,0)\
\
**@see** [getRot](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Models#getRot)\
, [getOffsetRot](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Models#getOffsetRot)\
,\
\
#### getOffsetRot\
\
* * *\
\
Returns the value that was used for `setOffsetRot`. Will be 0,0,0 when the script begins\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getOffsetRot()` | [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
\
print(head:getOffsetRot()) \--> vec(0,0,0)\
head:setOffsetRot(45, 0, 0)\
print(head:getOffsetRot()) \--> vec(45,0,0)\
\
**@see** [setOffsetRot](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Models#setOffsetRot)\
,\
\
#### setOffsetScale\
\
* * *\
\
Sets a scale value that will be multiplied with the ModelPart's scale.\
\
`nil` values are interpreted as 1. If a number is provided for x and both y and z are not defined, x will be used for all 3 axis.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `setOffsetScale(scale [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") )` | self ModelPart |\
| `setOffsetScale(scaleAll [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | self ModelPart |\
| `setOffsetScale(x [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) , y [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) , z [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | self ModelPart |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
\-- Double the size of the head\
head:setScale(2)\
\-- Half the size of the head\
head:setOffsetScale(0.5)\
\-- Results in no changes\
\-- I have no idea what this is used for\
\
#### getOffsetScale\
\
* * *\
\
Returns the value that was used for `setOffsetScale`. Always 1,1,1 when script begins.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getOffsetScale()` | [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
\
print(head:getOffsetScale()) \--> vec(1,1,1)\
head:setOffsetScale(2)\
print(head:getOffsetScale()) \--> vec(2,2,2)\
\
**@see** [setOffsetScale](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Models#setOffsetScale)\
,\
\
#### setOffsetPivot\
\
* * *\
\
Sets a value that will be added to the ModelPart's pivot point.\
\
`nil` values are interpreted as 0.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `setOffsetPivot(pivot [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") )` | self ModelPart |\
| `setOffsetPivot(x [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) , y [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) , z [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | self ModelPart |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
\
\-- If we assume that the Head cube is an 8x8x8 cube and offset the pivot up by 4,\
\-- then the head will rotate around the center of the cube instead of the neck\
head:setOffsetPivot(0, 4, 0)\
\-- Notice that we did not need to know the original pivot point to do this\
\
#### getOffsetPivot\
\
* * *\
\
Returns the value that was used for `setOffsetPivot`. Always 0,0,0 when script begins.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getOffsetPivot()` | [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
\
print(head:getOffsetPivot()) \--> vec(0,0,0)\
head:setOffsetPivot(0,4,0)\
print(head:getOffsetPivot()) \--> vec(0,4,0)\
\
**@see** [setOffsetPivot](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Models#setOffsetPivot)\
,\
\
#### setMatrix\
\
* * *\
\
Allows you to manually define the matrix used for positioning this ModelPart. Returns self for method chaining.\
\
Using `setPos`, `setRot`, `setScale`, `setPivot`, `setOffsetRot`, `setOffsetScale`, or `setOffsetPivot` will undo `setMatrix`\
\
Using `getPos`, `getRot`, `getScale`, `getPivot`, `getOffsetRot`, `getOffsetScale`, or `getOffsetPivot` will return invalid values while `setMatrix` is in effect.\
\
`getTruePos`, `getTrueRot`, `getTrueScale`, and `getTruePivot` are probably also affected, but nobody tested them yet.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `setMatrix(matrix [Matrix4](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vectors_and_Matrices "Vectors and Matrices") )` | self ModelPart |\
\
\-- no example provided\
\
#### getTruePos\
\
* * *\
\
Returns the position after all calculations are done. This includes `setPos` and the data from all playing Animations.\
\
This does not include ParentTypes or transformations applied from a parent part.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getTruePos()` | [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") |\
\
\-- no example provided\
\
#### getTrueRot\
\
* * *\
\
Returns the rotation after all calculations are done. This includes `setRot`, `setOffsetRot`, and the data from all playing Animations.\
\
This does not include ParentTypes or transformations applied from a parent part.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getTruePos()` | [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") |\
\
\-- no example provided\
\
#### getTrueScale\
\
* * *\
\
Returns the scale after all calculations are done. This includes `setScale`, `setOffsetScale`, and the data from all playing Animations.\
\
This does not include ParentTypes or transformations applied from a parent part.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getTrueScale()` | [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") |\
\
\-- no example provided\
\
#### getTruePivot\
\
* * *\
\
Returns the pivot point after all calculations are done. This includes `setPivot` and `setOffsetPivot`\
\
This does not include ParentTypes or transformations applied from a parent part.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getTruePivot()` | [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") |\
\
\-- no example provided\

### Visual manipulation\
\
Methods relating to modifying how a ModelPart looks\
\
todo: put anything related to renderType, textures, and other visual modifications in here\
\
#### setVisible\
\
* * *\
\
Sets if this ModelPart is visible or not. Children of this ModelPart will also be invisible while this part is invisible.\
\
A value of `nil` is interpreted as `true` on 0.1.4 and below, and `false` on 0.1.5 and above. This message will disappear ~if~ when 0.1.6 is released.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `setVisible(visible [boolean](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | self ModelPart |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
\
head:setVisible(false) \-- Bye bye Head!\
\
#### getVisible\
\
* * *\
\
Recursively goes up the ModelPart tree until it finds a ModelPart that is invisible, or the ModelPart is `models`\
\
In other words, if a parent part is invisible, this function returns `false`. If all parent parts are visible, this function will return `true` or `nil`. Kinda stupid. This is fixed in 0.1.5 to never return `nil`.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getVisible()` | [bool](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)<br> \| [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)<br> \[_until [0.1.5](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=0.1.5&action=edit&redlink=1 "0.1.5 (page does not exist)")<br>_\] |\
| `getVisible()` | [bool](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)<br> \[_since [0.1.5](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=0.1.5&action=edit&redlink=1 "0.1.5 (page does not exist)")<br>_\] |\
\
local root \= models.model.root.Head\
\
print(root.Head:getVisible()) \--> nil --< this is stupid\
root:setVisible(false) \-- Bye bye root!\
print(root.Head:getVisible()) \--> false\
root:setVisible(true) \-- Welcome back root!\
print(root.Head:getVisible()) \--> true --< aaaaaaaa\
\
#### setColor\
\
* * *\
\
Sets a value to multiply with all pixels on the ModelPart's texture. Children of this ModelPart inherit the color, multiplied with their own.\
\
1,1,1 multiplies all color channels by 1, resulting in the texture unchanged. 0,0,0 results in all channels being black.\
\
Expects values between 0 and 1. Numbers larger than 1 results in undocumented behaviour. `nil` values are interpreted as 1. If only `r` is defined as a number and both `g` and `b` are omitted, `r` is used for all 3 color channels.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `setColor(color [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") )` | self ModelPart |\
| `setColor(colorAll [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | self ModelPart |\
| `setColor(r [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) , g [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) , b [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | self ModelPart |\
\
local root \= models.model.root\
\-- Darken the entire model\
root:setColor(0.5,0.5,0.5)\
\-- Tint the Head red by reducing the other color channels.\
\-- Color is inherited from parents, so the effective color is (0.5, 0.45, 0.45)\
root.Head:setColor(1,0.7,0.7)\
\
\-- If you want to 'reset' a child's color value, extra work is needed.\
\
\-- Color is max red\
local color \= vec(1,0,0)\
local root \= models.model.root\
\-- root has color\
root:setColor(color)\
\-- Through magic and wizardry, this 'resets' the color of Head back to white, dispite it's parent having a non-white color\
root.Head:setColor(\-color + 2)\
\
#### getColor\
\
* * *\
\
Gets the value set by `setColor`. Returns 1,1,1 when script begins.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getColor()` | [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") |\
\
local root \= models.model.root\
root:setColor(0.5)\
print(root:getColor()) \--> (0.5, 0.5, 0.5)\
root.Head:setColor(1,0.7,0.7)\
// getColor is not recursive\
print(root.Head:getColor()) \--> (1, 0.7, 0.7)\
\
**@see** [setColor](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Models#setColor)\
,\
\
#### setOpacity\
\
* * *\
\
Sets the opacity of the ModelPart. Children of this ModelPart inherit the opacity, multiplied with their own.\
\
Minecraft has a minimum visible opacity of 0.1. Opacity values lower than 0.1 will not render at all. Needs verification.\
\
Only supported on [RenderTypes](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=RenderType&action=edit&redlink=1 "RenderType (page does not exist)")\
 that support translucency. The default primary RenderType is `TRANSLUCENT`, so most don't have to worry about it.\
\
Expects a value between 0 and 1.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `setOpacity(opacity [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | self ModelPart |\
\
local root \= models.model.root\
\-- Half opacity\
root:setOpacity(0.5)\
\-- Half of half opacity\
root.Head:setColor(0.5)\
\
#### getOpacity\
\
* * *\
\
Gets the value set by `setOpacity`. Returns 1 when script begins.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getOpacity()` | [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) |\
\
local root \= models.model.root\
root:setOpacity(0.5)\
print(root:getOpacity()) \--> 0.5\
root.Head:setOpacity(0.5)\
// getOpacity is not recursive\
print(root.Head:getOpacity()) \--> 0.5\
\
**@see** [setOpacity](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Models#setOpacity)\
,\
\
#### setLight\
\
* * *\
\
Overrides the lightlevels used to render the ModelPart. Children of this ModelPart inherit the lightlevel.\
\
Expects 2 values between 0 and 15, or `nil`. Providing `nil` will undo the override, allowing Minecraft to control the lightlevel again.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `setLight(light [Vector2](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2 "Vector2")  \| [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | self ModelPart |\
| `setLight(blockLight [integer](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)  \| [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) , skyLight [integer](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)  \| [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | self ModelPart |\
\
local root \= models.model.root\
\-- Max light\
root:setLight(15, 15)\
\
local root \= models.model.root\
\-- set light based on position (This is a fix for broken lighting on World parts)\
function events.tick()\
  local pos \= player:getPos()\
  local blockLight \= world.getBlockLightLevel(pos)\
  local skyLight \= world.getSkyLightLevel(pos)\
  root:setLight(blockLight, skyLight)\
end\
\
**@see** [player:getPos](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=PlayerAPI&action=edit&redlink=1 "PlayerAPI (page does not exist)")\
 [world.getBlockLightLevel](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=WorldAPI&action=edit&redlink=1 "WorldAPI (page does not exist)")\
 [world.getSkyLightLevel](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=WorldAPI&action=edit&redlink=1 "WorldAPI (page does not exist)")\
\
#### getLight\
\
* * *\
\
Gets the value set by `setLight`. Returns `nil` when script begins.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getLight()` | [Vector2](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2 "Vector2") |\
\
local root \= models.model.root\
\
print(root:getLight()) \--> nil\
\
root:setLight(12, 8)\
\
let light \= root:getLight()\
print(light) \--> vec(12, 8)\
print("BlockLightLevel -> ", light.x) \--> "BlockLightLevel -> 12"\
print("SkyLightLevel -> ", light.y) \--> "BlockLightLevel -> 8"\
\
**@see** [setLight](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Models#setLight)\
,\
\
#### setOverlay\
\
* * *\
\
Overrides the values used for rendering the red damage tint and the white creeper fuse effect. Really only useful for preventing the damage overlay from rendering on stuff like armor.\
\
Valid values for whiteOverlay: 0-15\
\
Valid values for hurtOverlay: 0-7\
\
whiteOverlay is a gradually increasing white tint from 0 - 15\
\
hurtOverlay is an unchanging red tint from 0 - 7.\
\
When set, hurtOverlay overrides whiteOverlay. For whiteOverlay to not be overriden, hurtOverlay needs to be 8 or more.\
\
Providing `nil` will undo the override, allowing Minecraft to control the overlay again.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `setOverlay(overlayVector [Vector2](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2 "Vector2")  \| [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | self ModelPart |\
| `setOverlay(whiteOverlay [integer](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)  \| [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) , hurtOverlay [integer](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | self ModelPart |\
\
local root \= models.model.root\
\-- Damage overlay\
root:setOverlay(0, 0)\
\-- Literally no difference\
root:setOverlay(0, 5)\
root:setOverlay(0, 7)\
\
\-- Doesnt work. Damage overlay overrides white\
root:setOverlay(15, 0)\
\
\-- This works. Max white overlay\
root:setOverlay(15, 15)\
\
\-- This can be used to for preventing the damage overlay on armor\
root:setOverlay(0, 15)\
\
\-- Give control back to Minecraft\
root:setOverlay(nil)\
\
#### getOverlay\
\
* * *\
\
Gets the value set by `setOverlay`. Returns `nil` when script begins.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getOverlay()` | [Vector2](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2 "Vector2") |\
\
local root \= models.model.root\
\
print(root:getOverlay()) \--> nil\
\
root:setOverlay(8, 15)\
\
let overlay \= root:getOverlay()\
print(overlay) \--> vec(8, 15)\
print("whiteOverlay -> ", overlay.x) \--> "whiteOverlay -> 8"\
print("hurtOverlay -> ", overlay.y) \--> "hurtOverlay -> 15"\
\
**@see** [setOverlay](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Models#setOverlay)\
,\

# Pings - FiguraMC

**Pings** are a networking feature in Figura that allows an avatar host to communicate additional information to viewers.

The following pages are related to pings:

*   The ping [tutorial](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Pings_(Tutorial) "Pings (Tutorial)")
    
*   [PingAPI](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=PingAPI&action=edit&redlink=1 "PingAPI (page does not exist)")
    , which registers and dispatches pings

Retrieved from "[https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Pings&oldid=260](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Pings&oldid=260)
"

# ConfigAPI - FiguraMC

(Redirected from [Config](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Config&redirect=no "Config")
)

This API is only available on the host.

For more information, see [Pings](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Pings "Pings")
.

The `ConfigAPI` allows storing and loading data between reloads of your avatar.

ConfigAPI is available as the global `config` variable.

Data types
----------

Only some data types are supported by ConfigAPI. All other data types will be converted to [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
. The supported data types are:

*   [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
    
*   [boolean](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
    
*   [string](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
    
*   [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
    
*   [table](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
    
*   all types of [Vector](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector "Vector")
    
*   all types of [Matrix](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vectors_and_Matrices "Vectors and Matrices")
    

ConfigAPI methods
-----------------

### Configuration switching

#### setName

* * *

Also available as `ConfigAPI:name`.

Sets the name of the configuration file to read and write data to. By default, the name of the configuration file is the same as the name of the currently loaded avatar.

| Arguments | Return Type |
| --- | --- |
| `setName(name [string](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | self ConfigAPI |

config:setName("my\_config\_file\_name")

#### getName

* * *

Returns the name of the active configuration file.

| Arguments | Return Type |
| --- | --- |
| `getName()` | [string](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) |

\-- Print the active configuration file's name.
print(config:getName())

### Reading and writing data

#### load

* * *

Read a saved value from the active configuration file (see [setName](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Config#setName)
) by key and return it. If no key is given, return all of the saved keys and values in a table.

| Arguments | Return Type |
| --- | --- |
| `load(key [string](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | [any](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)<br> \| [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) |
| `load()` | [table](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) |

\-- Print all saved values.
printTable(config:load())
\-- Print one specific value.
print(config:load("my\_value"))

#### save

* * *

Associate a key with a value in the active configuration file (see [setName](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Config#setName)
.) Only some types of values are allowed; see [Data Types](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Config#Data_Types)
 for details.

If [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
 is provided as the value, then the key is removed from the file.

| Arguments | Return Type |
| --- | --- |
| `save(key [string](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) , value [any](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)  \| [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | self ConfigAPI |

\-- Save a value to be used later.
config:save("my\_value", "Figura Wiki")

See also
--------

*   [Persisting Variables](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Tutorials/Persisting-Variables "Tutorials/Persisting-Variables")
     (tutorial)

# ConfigAPI - FiguraMC

This API is only available on the host.

For more information, see [Pings](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Pings "Pings")
.

The `ConfigAPI` allows storing and loading data between reloads of your avatar.

ConfigAPI is available as the global `config` variable.

Data types
----------

Only some data types are supported by ConfigAPI. All other data types will be converted to [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
. The supported data types are:

*   [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
    
*   [boolean](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
    
*   [string](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
    
*   [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
    
*   [table](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
    
*   all types of [Vector](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector "Vector")
    
*   all types of [Matrix](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vectors_and_Matrices "Vectors and Matrices")
    

ConfigAPI methods
-----------------

### Configuration switching

#### setName

* * *

Also available as `ConfigAPI:name`.

Sets the name of the configuration file to read and write data to. By default, the name of the configuration file is the same as the name of the currently loaded avatar.

| Arguments | Return Type |
| --- | --- |
| `setName(name [string](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | self ConfigAPI |

config:setName("my\_config\_file\_name")

#### getName

* * *

Returns the name of the active configuration file.

| Arguments | Return Type |
| --- | --- |
| `getName()` | [string](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) |

\-- Print the active configuration file's name.
print(config:getName())

### Reading and writing data

#### load

* * *

Read a saved value from the active configuration file (see [setName](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/ConfigAPI#setName)
) by key and return it. If no key is given, return all of the saved keys and values in a table.

| Arguments | Return Type |
| --- | --- |
| `load(key [string](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | [any](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)<br> \| [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) |
| `load()` | [table](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) |

\-- Print all saved values.
printTable(config:load())
\-- Print one specific value.
print(config:load("my\_value"))

#### save

* * *

Associate a key with a value in the active configuration file (see [setName](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/ConfigAPI#setName)
.) Only some types of values are allowed; see [Data Types](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/ConfigAPI#Data_Types)
 for details.

If [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
 is provided as the value, then the key is removed from the file.

| Arguments | Return Type |
| --- | --- |
| `save(key [string](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) , value [any](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)  \| [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | self ConfigAPI |

\-- Save a value to be used later.
config:save("my\_value", "Figura Wiki")

See also
--------

*   [Persisting Variables](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Tutorials/Persisting-Variables "Tutorials/Persisting-Variables")
     (tutorial)

# Vectors and Matrices - FiguraMC

(Redirected from [VectorsAPI](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=VectorsAPI&redirect=no "VectorsAPI")
)

This page is a [stub](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Stub "wikipedia:Wikipedia:Stub")
. You can help this wiki by [expanding it](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Vectors_and_Matrices&action=edit)

Not to be confused with [Vectors (Global)](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Vectors_(Global)&action=edit&redlink=1 "Vectors (Global) (page does not exist)")
, [Vector](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector "Vector")
, or [Matrices (Global)](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Matrices_(Global)&action=edit&redlink=1 "Matrices (Global) (page does not exist)")
.

Vectors and matrices at their core are **a set of numbers** that represent something (e.g. a Vector3 could represent a position in the world.)

Vectors are one-dimensional; for example, a [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3")
 holds 3 numbers. Vectors are most commonly used for representing the position and rotation of things.

Matrices are two-dimensional grids. All matrices are square, so a Matrix3 is a 3 by 3 grid of numbers. Matrices are most commonly used to represent transformations of vectors. For more in-depth information, see [the Wikipedia article on transformation matrices](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Transformation_matrix "wikipedia:Transformation matrix")
.

Vectors
-------

Many functions that take in a vector will also take in the same amount of numbers and internally convert it into a Vector.

Vectors come in 3 types: Vector2, Vector3, and Vector4. The number refers to the size of the vector (Vector4 has 4 numbers, etc.) You can create a vector by using the global method `vec` as shown:

*   vec(x [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
    , y [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
    , z [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
     | [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
    , w [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
     | [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
    )

This method will return a vector based on how many arguments you input.

Matrices
--------

Matrices are a set of vectors, which are normally used to change where models are, how they look, etc.

# EventsAPI - FiguraMC

Not to be confused with [Event](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Event "Event")
.

Events is a global which contains every [Event](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Event_(type) "Event (type)")
, which are fired when certain things happen. For example, if you want to count ticks, you can use the tick or world tick event.

local tick \= 0

\-- Register event
function events.TICK()
  tick \= tick + 1
end
\-- or
events.TICK:register(function()
  tick \= tick + 1
end)

Note that not everyone needs to count ticks

Methods
-------

| Method | Description |
| --- | --- |
| [getEvents](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/EventsAPI#getEvents) | Returns a table of every event |

Fields
------

| Event | Description |
| --- | --- |
| [ENTITY\_INIT](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/ENTITY_INIT&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/ENTITY INIT (page does not exist)") | Runs when the player is loaded |
| [TICK](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/TICK&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/TICK (page does not exist)") | Runs every tick the player is rendered |
| [WORLD\_TICK](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/WORLD_TICK&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/WORLD TICK (page does not exist)") | Runs every tick the world is rendered |
| [RENDER](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/RENDER&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/RENDER (page does not exist)") | Runs every frame the player is rendered |
| [POST\_RENDER](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/POST_RENDER&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/POST RENDER (page does not exist)") | Runs every frame AFTER the player is rendered |
| [WORLD\_RENDER](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/WORLD_RENDER&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/WORLD RENDER (page does not exist)") | Runs every frame the world is rendered |
| [POST\_WORLD\_RENDER](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/POST_WORLD_RENDER&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/POST WORLD RENDER (page does not exist)") | Runs every frame AFTER the world is rendered |
| [SKULL\_RENDER](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/SKULL_RENDER&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/SKULL RENDER (page does not exist)") | Runs every frame for every skull when the skull is rendered. |
| [ARROW\_RENDER](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/ARROW_RENDER&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/ARROW RENDER (page does not exist)") | Runs every frame for every arrow when rendered. |
| [TRIDENT\_RENDER](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/TRIDENT_RENDER&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/TRIDENT RENDER (page does not exist)") | Runs every frame for every trident when rendered. |
| [ITEM\_RENDER](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/ITEM_RENDER&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/ITEM RENDER (page does not exist)") | Runs every frame for every item when rendered. |
| [CHAT\_SEND\_MESSAGE](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/CHAT_SEND_MESSAGE&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/CHAT SEND MESSAGE (page does not exist)") | Runs every time the player sends something in chat, including commands. Allows for changing the message |
| [CHAT\_RECEIVE\_MESSAGE](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/CHAT_RECEIVE_MESSAGE&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/CHAT RECEIVE MESSAGE (page does not exist)") | Runs every time the player receives something in chat. Allows for changing the message |
| [MOUSE\_SCROLL](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/MOUSE_SCROLL&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/MOUSE SCROLL (page does not exist)") | Runs every time the mouse is scrolled. Allows for cancelling the vanilla function |
| [MOUSE\_MOVE](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/MOUSE_MOVE&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/MOUSE MOVE (page does not exist)") | Runs every time the mouse is moved. Allows for cancelling the vanilla function |
| [MOUSE\_PRESS](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/MOUSE_PRESS&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/MOUSE PRESS (page does not exist)") | Runs every time the mouse is clicked. Allows for cancelling the vanilla function |
| [KEY\_PRESS](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/KEY_PRESS&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/KEY PRESS (page does not exist)") | Runs every time a key is pressed. Allows for cancelling the vanilla function |
| [CHAR\_TYPED](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/CHAR_TYPED&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/CHAR TYPED (page does not exist)") | Runs every time a character is typed. |
| [USE\_ITEM](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/USE_ITEM&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/USE ITEM (page does not exist)") | Runs every time an item is used by the player. |
| [ON\_PLAY\_SOUND](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/ON_PLAY_SOUND&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/ON PLAY SOUND (page does not exist)") | Runs every time a sound is played |
| [RESOURCE\_RELOAD](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/RESOURCE_RELOAD&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/RESOURCE RELOAD (page does not exist)") | Runs every time resources are reloaded |
| [TOTEM](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/TOTEM&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/TOTEM (page does not exist)") | Runs every time a totem of undying is activated |
| [DAMAGE](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Events/DAMAGE&action=edit&redlink=1 "Events/DAMAGE (page does not exist)") | Runs whenever the player takes damage |

Methods
-------

#### getEvents

* * *

Returns a table of every event

\-- Example function to clear all events
function clearEvents()
  for \_, v in pairs(events:getEvents()) do
    v:clear()
  end
end

Retrieved from "[https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=EventsAPI&oldid=569](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=EventsAPI&oldid=569)
"
