# Event (type) - FiguraMC

(Redirected from [Event](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Event&redirect=no "Event")
)

Not to be confused with [Events](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Events "Events")
.

The event type is used for events such as `events.TICK`. To create an event function, use one of the following.

 local tick \= 0
function events.WORLD\_TICK()
  tick \= tick + 1
end
\-- OR
local tick \= 0
events.WORLD\_TICK:register(function()
  tick \= tick + 1
end, "TICK\_COUNTER")

Methods
-------

| Method | Description |
| --- | --- |
| [remove](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Event#remove) | Takes in a [string](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)<br> with the name of the event, and removes it, stopping it from being called |
| [clear](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Event#clear) | Clears the event of all methods |
| [register](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Event#register) | Takes in a [function](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)<br> to run when the event is fired, with an optional name argument ([string](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)<br>) |
| [getRegisteredCount](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Event#getRegisteredCount) | Returns the amount of functions registered, with an optional name argument ([string](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)<br>) |

#### remove

* * *

Removes a function from an event, returning how many were removed

Overloads:

| Arguments | Return |
| --- | --- |
| name: [string](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) | [integer](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) |
| function: [function](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) | [integer](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) |

local tick \= 0
function tickThing()
  tick \= tick + 1
  print("tick " .. tick)
  if tick \> 5 then
    events.TICK:remove("thing:)
  end
end
events.TICK:register(tickThing, "tickThing")

#### clear

* * *

Similar to remove, but removes every event

Overloads:

| Arguments | Return |
| --- | --- |
| none | [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) |

\-- Example function to clear all events
function clearEvents()
  for \_, v in pairs(events:getEvents()) do
    v:clear()
  end
end

#### register

Registers a function to an event

Overloads:

| Arguments | Return |
| --- | --- |
| func: [function](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)<br>, name: [string](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) | Event |
| func: [function](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) | Event |

local fps \= 0
events.RENDER:register(function()
  fps \= client.getFPS()
end)

#### getRegisteredCount

Gets the number of registered functions in an event, optionally filtering by name

Overloads:

| Arguments | Return |
| --- | --- |
| name: [Integer](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) | Event |
| none | [Integer](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) |

local fps \= 0
events.RENDER:register(function()
  fps \= client.getFPS()
end)

# Vectors and Matrices - FiguraMC

(Redirected from [Matrix4](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Matrix4&redirect=no "Matrix4")
)

This page is a [stub](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Stub "wikipedia:Wikipedia:Stub")
. You can help this wiki by [expanding it](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Vectors_and_Matrices&action=edit)

Not to be confused with [Vectors (Global)](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Vectors_(Global)&action=edit&redlink=1 "Vectors (Global) (page does not exist)")
, [Vector](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector "Vector")
, or [Matrices (Global)](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Matrices_(Global)&action=edit&redlink=1 "Matrices (Global) (page does not exist)")
.

Vectors and matrices at their core are **a set of numbers** that represent something (e.g. a Vector3 could represent a position in the world.)

Vectors are one-dimensional; for example, a [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3")
 holds 3 numbers. Vectors are most commonly used for representing the position and rotation of things.

Matrices are two-dimensional grids. All matrices are square, so a Matrix3 is a 3 by 3 grid of numbers. Matrices are most commonly used to represent transformations of vectors. For more in-depth information, see [the Wikipedia article on transformation matrices](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Transformation_matrix "wikipedia:Transformation matrix")
.

Vectors
-------

Many functions that take in a vector will also take in the same amount of numbers and internally convert it into a Vector.

Vectors come in 3 types: Vector2, Vector3, and Vector4. The number refers to the size of the vector (Vector4 has 4 numbers, etc.) You can create a vector by using the global method `vec` as shown:

*   vec(x [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
    , y [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
    , z [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
     | [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
    , w [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
     | [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
    )

This method will return a vector based on how many arguments you input.

Matrices
--------

Matrices are a set of vectors, which are normally used to change where models are, how they look, etc.

# Vector2 - FiguraMC

For general information on vectors, see [Vector](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector "Vector")
 and [Vectors and Matrices](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vectors_and_Matrices "Vectors and Matrices")
.

A **Vector2** is a [vector](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector "Vector")
 that contains 2 numbers.

Methods
-------

| Method | Brief description |
| --- | --- |
| [length](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#length) | Computes the length of the vector. |
| [lengthSquared](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#lengthSquared) | Computes the squared length of the vector. |
| [dot](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#dot) | Computes the dot product between vectors. |
| [add](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#add)<br> _in-place_ | Adds vectors. |
| [subtract](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#subtract)<br> _in-place_ | Subtracts vectors. |
| [offset](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#offset)<br> _in-place_ | Adds a number to each component of the vector. |
| [multiply](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#multiply)<br> _in-place_ | Performs component multiplication. |
| [transform](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#transform)<br> _in-place_ | Transforms a vector with a matrix. |
| [divide](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#divide)<br> _in-place_ | Performs component division. |
| [reduce](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#reduce)<br> _in-place_ | Runs the modulo operation on each component of the vector. |
| [scale](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#scale)<br> _in-place_ | Multiplies each component of the vector by a number. |
| [normalize](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#normalize)<br> _in-place_ | Normalizes the vector, making its length 1. |
| [clampLength](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#clampLength)<br> _in-place_ | Applies bounds to the length of the vector, scaling as needed. |
| [clamped](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#clamped) | Returns a new copy of this vector with [clampLength](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#clampLength)<br> applied. |
| [normalized](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#normalized) | Returns a new, normalized copy of the vector. |
| [toRad](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#toRad) | Returns a copy of this vector, converted to radians. |
| [toDeg](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#toDeg) | Returns a copy of this vector, converted to degrees. |
| [floor](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#floor)<br> _in-place_ | Floors the components of the vector. |
| [ceil](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#ceil)<br> _in-place_ | Ceilings the components of the vector. |
| [copy](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#copy) | Returns a copy of this vector. |
| [set](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#set)<br> _in-place_ | Assigns the values from another vector to this one. |
| [reset](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#reset)<br> _in-place_ | Sets the components of this vector to 0. |
| [applyFunc](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#applyFunc)<br> _in-place_ | Apply a function to the components of this vector. |
| [augmented](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#augmented) | Convert this vector into a [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3")<br> by appending a number. |

Fields
------

| Field | Brief description |
| --- | --- |
| [\_](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#field_zero) | Always 0. |
| [x](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#field_x)<br>, [r](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#field_r)<br>, `[1]` | First component. |
| [y](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#field_y)<br>, [g](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#field_g)<br>, `[2]` | Second component. |

Operators
---------

| Operator | Brief description |
| --- | --- |
| [(vector + vector)](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#meta_add_vv) | Add two vectors. |
| [(vector + number) _comm._](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#meta_add_vn) | Add the number to each component of the vector. |
| [(-vector)](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#meta_unm) | Negate the vector. |
| [(vector - vector)](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#meta_sub_vv) | Subtract two vectors. |
| [(vector - number)](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#meta_sub_vn) | Subtract the number from each component of the vector. |
| [(number - vector)](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#meta_sub_nv) | Negate the vector, then add the number to each component. |
| [(vector \* vector)](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#meta_mul_vv) | Multiply (component-wise) two vectors. |
| [(vector \* number) _comm._](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#meta_mul_vn) | Scale the vector. |
| [(vector \* matrix)](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#meta_mul_vm) | Transform the vector using the matrix. |
| [(vector / vector)](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#meta_div_vv) | Divide (component-wise) two vectors. |
| [(vector / number)](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#meta_div_vn) | Scale the vector by (1/number). |
| [(#vector)](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#meta_len) | Number of components in the vector. |
| [(vector < vector)](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#meta_lt) | Component-wise less than. |
| [(vector <= vector)](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#meta_le) | Component-wise less than or equal. |
| [tostring(vector)](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#meta_tostring) | Result of `tostring(vector)`. |

Methods
-------

### Math operations

Mathematical operations that apply to all vectors, such as computing their length

#### length

* * *

Mathematical definition

Computes the [Euclidean norm](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norm_(mathematics)#Euclidean_norm "wikipedia:Norm (mathematics)")
 of the vector.

Computes the length of a vector.

| Arguments | Return Type |
| --- | --- |
| `length()` | [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) |

#### lengthSquared

* * *

Computes the length of a vector, squared. Due to the nature of the length calculation, this is a little bit faster than [`length`](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#length)
.

| Arguments | Return Type |
| --- | --- |
| `lengthSquared()` | [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) |

#### dot

* * *

Computes the [dot product](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/dot_product "wikipedia:dot product")
 between two vectors. The argument must be the same type as the target vector.

| Arguments | Return Type |
| --- | --- |
| `dot(Vector2 other)` | [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) |

#### add

* * *

Mathematical definition

Performs [vector addition](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Euclidean_vector#Addition_and_subtraction "wikipedia:Euclidean vector")
 with another vector, storing the result in this vector.

Adds the values from this vector and another vector of the same size, and writes them to this vector. To create a new instance from the sum, see [\+ (operator)](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#meta_add_vv)
.

| Arguments | Return Type |
| --- | --- |
| `add(Vector2 other)` | self Vector2 |

#### subtract

* * *

Mathematical definition

Performs [vector subtraction](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Euclidean_vector#Addition_and_subtraction "wikipedia:Euclidean vector")
 with another vector (in the order **this - other**), storing the result in this vector.

Subtracts the passed vector of the same size from this vector, and writes the result to this vector. To create a new instance from the difference, see [\- (operator)](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#meta_sub_vv)
.

| Arguments | Return Type |
| --- | --- |
| `subtract(Vector2 other)` | self Vector2 |

#### offset

* * *

Adds _factor_ to all components of this vector. To create a new instance from the result, see [\+ (operator)](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#meta_add_vn)
 or [\- (operator)](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#meta_sub_vn)
.

| Arguments | Return Type |
| --- | --- |
| `offset([number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)  factor)` | self Vector2 |

#### multiply

* * *

Multiplies vectors of the same size by multiplying their components. The result is written to this vector.

| Arguments | Return Type |
| --- | --- |
| `multiply(Vector2 other)` | self Vector2 |

#### transform

* * *

Mathematical definition

[Multiplies](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Matrix_multiplication#Matrix_times_vector "wikipedia:Matrix multiplication")
 the provided matrix with this vector, in the order _M \* V_, and writes the resulting vector to this vector.

Applies a matrix transformation to this vector. Equivalent to multiplying the matrix by the vector. The matrix must be the same size as the vector{{#ifVector2|.|; the following are valid:}}

  

| Arguments | Return Type |
| --- | --- |
| `transform([Matrix2](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vectors_and_Matrices "Vectors and Matrices")  mat)` | self Vector2 |

#### divide

* * *

Divides vectors of the same size by dividing their components. The result is written to this vector.

| Arguments | Return Type |
| --- | --- |
| `divide(Vector2 other)` | self Vector2 |

#### reduce

* * *

For each component in this vector, perform the [positive modulo](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/modulo "wikipedia:modulo")
 operation on it and the equivalent component in the other vector.

| Arguments | Return Type |
| --- | --- |
| `reduce(Vector2 other)` | self Vector2 |

#### scale

* * *

Multiplies each component in this vector by _factor_.

| Arguments | Return Type |
| --- | --- |
| `scale([number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)  factor)` | self Vector2 |

#### normalize

* * *

[Normalizes](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Unit_vector "wikipedia:Unit vector")
 this vector in-place. After this operation, the [length](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#length)
 of the vector will be 1, **unless the length is currently 0**. If this vector's length is 0, then no normalization will occur.

| Arguments | Return Type |
| --- | --- |
| `normalize()` | self Vector2 |

#### clampLength

* * *

[Scales](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#scale)
 this vector such that its [length](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#length)
 is within the bounds specified by _minLength_ and _maxLength_. **If this vector's length is 0**, no scaling will be performed, even if _minLength_ is greater than 0. If this vector's length is already within the specified bounds, no scaling will be performed.

Both _minLength_ and _maxLength_ can be omitted or set to [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
, resulting in no lower or upper bound on the length of the vector.

| Arguments | Return Type |
| --- | --- |
| `clampLength([number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)  \| [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)  minLength, [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)  \| [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)  maxLength)` | self Vector2 |

#### clamped

* * *

[Copies](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#copy)
 this vector, then clamps its length. See [clampLength](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#clampLength)
 for details.

| Arguments | Return Type |
| --- | --- |
| `clamped([number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)  \| [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)  minLength, [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)  \| [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)  maxLength)` | new Vector2 |

#### normalized

* * *

[Copies](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#copy)
 this vector, then normalizes it. See [normalize](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#normalize)
 for details.

| Arguments | Return Type |
| --- | --- |
| `normalized()` | new Vector2 |

#### toRad

* * *

Returns a [copy](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#copy)
 of this vector, [scaled](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#scale)
 by a factor of _(pi / 180)_. If this vector represents a rotation in degrees, the result will be a rotation in radians.

_See also [toDeg](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#toDeg)
._

| Arguments | Return Type |
| --- | --- |
| `toRad()` | new Vector2 |

#### toDeg

* * *

Returns a [copy](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#copy)
 of this vector, [scaled](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#scale)
 by a factor of _(180 / pi)_. If this vector represents a rotation in radians, the result will be a rotation in degrees.

_See also [toRad](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#toRad)
._

| Arguments | Return Type |
| --- | --- |
| `toDeg()` | new Vector2 |

#### floor

* * *

Returns a [copy](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#copy)
 of this vector with every component floored.

| Arguments | Return Type |
| --- | --- |
| `floor()` | new Vector2 |

  

#### ceil

* * *

Returns a [copy](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#copy)
 of this vector with every component ceiling-ed.

| Arguments | Return Type |
| --- | --- |
| `ceil()` | new Vector2 |

### Utility methods

#### copy

* * *

Creates a copy of this vector. Creating a copy will make a new Vector with the same size and values, but which is disconnected from the original. This means that methods like [set](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#set)
 or [add](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#add)
 which modify the vector they are called with will not modify copies.

| Arguments | Return Type |
| --- | --- |
| `copy()` | new Vector2 |

#### set

* * *

Assigns the values from another vector of the same size to this vector in place. To create a new instance, see [copy](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#copy)
.

| Arguments | Return Type |
| --- | --- |
| `set(Vector2 other)` | self Vector2 |

#### reset

* * *

Sets all the components of this vector to 0.

| Arguments | Return Type |
| --- | --- |
| `reset()` | self Vector2 |

#### applyFunc

* * *

Calls the provided function _f_ on every component, and sets this vector's components to the return values of the function.

The function receives the following values as arguments: first, the value as a [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
, then the index ([integer](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
, 1 is x, 2 is y, etc.) The function is expected to return a [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
.

| Arguments | Return Type |
| --- | --- |
| `applyFunc([function](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)  f)` | self Vector2 |

local A \= vec(1, 2, 3)
\-- cube the values
A:applyFunc(function(value, index) return value\*value\*value end)
print(A) \-- {1, 8, 27}

### Vector2 methods

#### augmented

* * *

Converts this Vector2 into a [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3")
 using the provided number as the third component.

| Arguments | Return Type |
| --- | --- |
| `augmented([number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)  d)` | [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") |

Fields
------

### Swizzling

Swizzling is available for all vector types. For details, see [Swizzling](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector#Swizzling "Vector")
.

### `_`

Read-only [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
. Always 0. Attempting to write to this field will have no effect.

### Vector2 fields

#### x, r, 1

* * *

Read/write [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
. The first component of the vector.

#### y, g, 2

* * *

Read/write [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
. The second component of the vector.

Operators
---------

Lua operators, such as `+`, `-`, and `*`, apply to vectors and have different results.

#### \+ (operator)

##### With two vectors

* * *

Adds the values from this vector and another vector of the same size. The result is a _new_ vector of the same size which holds the sum.

| Left | Right | Result |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Vector2 | Vector2 | new Vector2 |

local a \= vec(1, 2, 3)
local b \= vec(4, 4, 6)
print(a + b, a, b) \-- {5, 6, 9}  {1, 2, 3}  {4, 4, 6}

##### With a vector and number

Operator is commutative and has the same result regardless of order.

The result is a new vector of the same size which holds the result of adding the number to all components of this vector.

| Left | Right | Result |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Vector2 | [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) | new Vector2 |
| [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) | Vector2 | new Vector2 |

#### \- (operator)

##### As a unary operator

* * *

Returns a new vector of the same size, but all the components negated. Effectively the same as `[*](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#meta_mul_vn)  -1`.

| Operand | Result |
| --- | --- |
| Vector2 | new Vector2 |

##### With two vectors

* * *

Mathematical definition

Performs [vector subtraction](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Euclidean_vector#Addition_and_subtraction "wikipedia:Euclidean vector")
 with another vector, and creates a new vector from the result.

Subtracts the right vector from the left vector. The result is a _new_ vector of the same size which holds the difference.

| Left | Right | Result |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Vector2 | Vector2 | new Vector2 |

local a \= vec(1, 2, 3)
local b \= vec(4, 4, 6)
print(b \- a, a, b) \-- {3, 2, 3}  {1, 2, 3}  {4, 4, 6}

##### With a vector and a number

Only applies when the number is on the **right** side of the operator.

Returns a new vector of the same size containing the result of subtracting the number from all components of the vector.

| Left | Right | Result |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Vector2 | [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) | new Vector2 |

##### With a number and a vector

Only applies when the number is on the **left** side of the operator.

Returns a new vector of the same size containing the result of negating all of the components of the vector, then [adding](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#meta_add_vn)
 the number. In effect, `number - vector == (-vector) + number`.

| Left | Right | Result |
| --- | --- | --- |
| [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) | Vector2 | new Vector2 |

#### \* (operator)

##### With two vectors

* * *

Returns a new vector of the same size containing the result of [multiplying](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#multiply)
 the vectors together (component multiplication.)

| Left | Right | Result |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Vector2 | Vector2 | new Vector2 |

##### With a vector and a number

Operator is commutative and has the same result regardless of order.

Returns a new vector of the same size containing the result of [scaling](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#scale)
 the vector by the number (scalar multiplication.)

| Left | Right | Result |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Vector2 | [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) | new Vector2 |
| [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) | Vector2 | new Vector2 |

##### With a vector and a matrix

This definition only applies if the vector is on the left side. If the vector is on the right side, see [the associated operator on the matrix](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Matrix2#meta_mul_mv "Matrix2")
.

Returns a new vector of the same size containing the result of [transforming](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#transform)
 the vector with the matrix.

| Left | Right | Result |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Vector2 | [Matrix2](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vectors_and_Matrices "Vectors and Matrices") | new Vector2 |

#### / (operator)

##### With two vectors

* * *

Returns a new vector of the same size containing the result of [dividing](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#divide)
 the left vector by the right vector (component division.)

| Left | Right | Result |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Vector2 | Vector2 | new Vector2 |

##### With a vector and a number

Only applies when the number is on the **right** side of the operator. There is no definition with the number on the left side of the operator.

Returns a new vector of the same size containing the result of [scaling](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2#scale)
 the vector by the [reciprocal](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Multiplicative_inverse "wikipedia:Multiplicative inverse")
 of the number.

| Left | Right | Result |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Vector2 | [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) | new Vector2 |

#### \# (operator)

* * *

Returns the number of components in this vector(2)

| Operand | Result |
| --- | --- |
| Vector2 | `2` |

#### < (operator)

* * *

Returns `true` if **all** of the components of the left vector are strictly less than the corresponding components of the right vector.

| Left | Right | Result |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Vector2 | Vector2 | [boolean](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) |

local A \= vec(1, 2, 3)
local B \= vec(4, 5, 6)
local C \= vec(4, 1, 6)
print(A < B) \-- true
print(B < C) \-- false

#### <= (operator)

* * *

Returns `true` if **all** of the components of the left vector are strictly less than or equal to the corresponding components of the right vector.

| Left | Right | Result |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Vector2 | Vector2 | [boolean](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) |

local A \= vec(1, 2, 3)
local B \= vec(4, 5, 6)
local C \= vec(1, 2, 3)
print(A <= B) \-- true
print(B <= C) \-- true

#### tostring return value

* * *

Converts the vector to a string representing its components.

| Operand | Result |
| --- | --- |
| Vector2 | [string](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) |

Retrieved from "[https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Vector2&oldid=737](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Vector2&oldid=737)
"

# Print - FiguraMC

Figura's print function is simlar to lua's print function, but has a couple extra features:

*   You can hover over a table to view it's children
    *   This includes userdata such as [Vector3s](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3")
        

Retrieved from "[https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Print&oldid=814](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Print&oldid=814)
"

---

# parseJson - FiguraMC

| Arguments | Returns |
| --- | --- |
| JSON: [string](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) | [table](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) |

Deserializes a JSON string into a table.  
See [toJson](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/ToJson "ToJson")

---

# ModelPart - FiguraMC

A ModelPart represents a Cube, Mesh, or Group from Blockbench.

Via scripting, ModelParts can be modified dynamically to achieve whatever visuals you need (limited to Minecraft's rendering engine)

Accessing ModelParts
--------------------

_From [:ModelPart Indexing](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/ModelPart_Indexing "ModelPart Indexing")
 ([edit](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=ModelPart_Indexing&action=edit)
)_

  
When Figura loads your avatar, all the model files in your avatar are organized into a tree. The starting point of this tree is called `models`. All of the parts of your model, including cubes, meshes, and groups from your Blockbench models, as well as folders in your avatar and the model files themselves are converted to ModelParts and part of this tree.

The name `models` does not refer to any specific model file in your avatar. Instead, model files are created as children of the `models` folder. **If your Blockbench model is inside a subfolder of your avatar**, that folder becomes a child of `models`, and the model file becomes a child of the subfolder.

![](https://wiki.figuramc.org/images/5/55/BBModel.png)`model.bbmodel`

![](https://wiki.figuramc.org/images/7/77/BBGroup.png)root

![](https://wiki.figuramc.org/images/7/77/BBGroup.png)Head

![](https://wiki.figuramc.org/images/1/1c/BBCube.png)Head

![](https://wiki.figuramc.org/images/1/1c/BBCube.png)HeadLayer

![](https://wiki.figuramc.org/images/7/77/BBGroup.png)RightArm

![](https://wiki.figuramc.org/images/1/1c/BBCube.png)RightArm

![](https://wiki.figuramc.org/images/1/1c/BBCube.png)RightArmLayer

![](https://wiki.figuramc.org/images/1/1c/BBCube.png)Cool Name

![](https://wiki.figuramc.org/images/7/77/BBGroup.png)Cool Group

![](https://wiki.figuramc.org/images/1/1c/BBCube.png)cube

To access a child part, _index_ the parent part with the name of the child part.

There are two ways to _index_ something in Lua. The first way is by using dots:

`models.model.root.Head`

This code sample first gets the `model` part (a file named `model.bbmodel`) and then the `Head` group inside it. The name of the cube, mesh, group, folder, or file needs to be within the quotes. To access deeper parts (for example, a `HeadLayer` cube within the `Head` group), add more dots and names:

`models.model.root.Head.HeadLayer`

The second way to index is longer, and uses square brackets and quotes (`[""]`) to separate the names. **This method is required if the name of a part contains characters that aren't letters, numbers, or underscores**; this includes _names with spaces_, like `Right Arm`.

When using brackets to index, place the name **between the quotes**, and **don't include a period before it**:

*   `models["model"]["root"]["Cool Name"]` ✓ Correct
    
*   `models.model.root["Cool Name"]` ✓ Correct - both brackets and dots can be mixed together!
    
*   `models.model.root.["Cool Name"]` ✗ Incorrect: **don't put a dot `.` before the bracket `[`.**\
    \
*   `models.model.root[Cool Name]` ✗ Incorrect: **name in brackets is missing a set of quotes**\
    \
\
To return to using dots for indexing after using brackets, place the dot after the closing bracket:\
\
*   `models.model.root["Cool Group"].cube` ✓ Correct\
    \
*   `models.model.root["Cool Group"]cube` ✗ Incorrect: **missing dot `.` after bracket**\
    \
\
### A note on model files in folders\
\
If your Blockbench model file is within a folder in your avatar, the _folder_ will become a part of the ModelPart tree. That means that if a model file named `player.bbmodel` is located in a folder named `models`, the model file has to be accessed with `models.models.player` (or `models["models"]["player"]`.)\
\
If you later want to use animations from a model, folders affect the indexing into the `animations` table too - but the system is a little different.\
\
Instead of indexing the folder and then the file, _combine each folder name and the file name with a period `.` and index with the combined name_, even if the names of the folders and files contain special characters. For example, to get the animations from the `model 2.bbmodel` file in the `main models` folder:\
\
![](https://wiki.figuramc.org/images/f/f1/FSFolderClosed.png)`main models`\
\
![](https://wiki.figuramc.org/images/5/55/BBModel.png)`model 2.bbmodel`\
\
animations\["main models.model 2"\]\
\
ParentTypes\
-----------\
\
In Figura, a [ParentType](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/ParentType "ParentType")\
 is applied to a ModelPart causing the ModelPart to behave in a predefined way. This behavior includes acting as a vanilla part like the Head or LeftLeg, moving the rendering of special parts like held items, armor, or parrots, and binding the ModelPart to the World instead of the Player.\
\
ParentTypes can either be applied in Blockbench itself or via script.\
\
### ParentTypes via BlockBench\
\
To define a ParentType in Blockbench, the name of a Group must begin with a case-sensitive ParentType.\
\
For example, the `Head` ParentType causes the ModelPart to move and rotate like the vanilla Head. If you name a Group the following, it will have this ParentType:\
\
*   Head\
*   HEAD\
*   Head2\
*   HeadPhones\
\
If you name a group the following, **it will not** have the `Head` ParentType:\
\
*   head => 'head' is not a valid ParentType. Capitalization matters!\
*   BigHead => Does not begin with ParentType\
*   HeAd => 'HeAd' is not a valid ParentType. Capitalization matters!\
\
Do note that some English words naturally start with a ParentType which can cause unintended behavior!\
\
For example, the word "Guitar". Seems innocent, right? Well, "Guitar" starts with "Gui", and "Gui" is an alias for the ParentType `Hud`, a ParentType that binds the ModelPart to the Heads Up Display where the hotbar and inventory reside. This causes the ModelPart to not be visible, as [`Hud` parts have special rules](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=ParentType/Hud&action=edit&redlink=1 "ParentType/Hud (page does not exist)")\
. Be careful!\
\
Note: ParentTypes are sometimes called Keywords by legacy Figura users\
\
### ParentTypes via Script\
\
Calling the `setParentType` on _any_ ModelPart will override it's ParentType.\
\
Simply [access](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/ModelPart#Accessing_ModelParts)\
 the ModelPart, then call `setParentType` on it, passing in the ParentType as a string.\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
head:setParentType("RightArm")\
\
To remove a ParentType from a ModelPart, call `setParentType` with the string `"None"`\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
head:setParentType("None")\
\
ModelParts **do not** remember their original ParentType! If you need a ModelPart's original ParentType, store it in a variable for later:\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
local headParentType \= head:getParentType()\
head:setParentType("None")\
\
ModelPart methods\
-----------------\
\
### ModelPart properties\
\
Read-only properties of a ModelPart\
\
#### getName\
\
* * *\
\
Returns the name of this ModelPart. ModelParts can have duplicate names.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getName()` | [string](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
print(head:getName()) \--> "Head"\
\
#### getType\
\
* * *\
\
Returns the original type of this ModelPart. Can be `Cube`, `Mesh`, or `Group`. BBModels and folders are considered Groups. Cubes with no texture data are also considered Groups, as with no texture data their face data is stripped.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getType()` | `"Cube" \| "Mesh" \| "Group"` |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
print(head:getType()) \--> "Group"\
\
### Editing ModelPart hierarchy\
\
Methods relating to getting other ModelParts and manipulating the ModelPart tree\
\
#### getParent\
\
* * *\
\
Returns the parent of this ModelPart, or `nil` if this is `models` or a loose ModelPart created via script.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getParent()` | ModelPart \| [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
print(head:getParent()) \--> ModelPart(root)\
\
#### getChildren\
\
* * *\
\
Returns an array containing all children of this ModelPart\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getChildren()` | ModelPart\[\] |\
\
local root \= models.model.root\
printTable(root:getChildren()) \--\[\[\
ModelPart(Head), \
ModelPart(Body), \
ModelPart(RightArm), \
ModelPart(LeftArm), \
ModelPart(RightLeg), \
ModelPart(LeftLeg),\
\]\]\--\
\
#### isChildOf\
\
* * *\
\
Recursively checks if this child is a decedent of the provided ModelPart.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `isChildOf(part ModelPart)` | [boolean](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) |\
\
local model \= models.model\
local head \= model.root.Head\
print(head:isChildOf(model)) \--> true\
\
#### copy\
\
* * *\
\
Copies the data of this ModelPart, assigning it a new name, then returning it. The new name has nothing to do with ParentTypes. The children of the copy are references to the original ModelPart's children. Extra work needs to be done to recursively copy it's children. The [addChild](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/ModelPart#ModelPart_addChild)\
 method can then be used to add the copy to the ModelPart tree.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `copy(newName [string](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | ModelPart |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
\
local headCopy \= head:copy("NewHead")\
print(headCopy) \--> ModelPart(NewHead)\
\
\-- The parentType is copied with the ModelPart\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
\
local headCopy \= head:copy("NewHead")\
print(headCopy:getParentType()) \--> "Head"\
\
headCopy:setParentType("None")\
print(headCopy:getParentType()) \--> "None"\
\
**@see** [setParentType](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/ModelPart#setParentType)\
,, [getParentType](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/ModelPart#getParentType)\
,\
\
\-- Extra work is needed to deep copy a ModelPart's children as well\
local function deepCopy(model)\
    local copy \= model:copy(model:getName())\
    for \_, child in pairs(copy:getChildren()) do\
        copy:removeChild(child):addChild(deepCopy(child))\
    end\
    return copy\
end\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
local headCube \= head.Head\
\
\-- headCopyA contains references to head's children because it is a shallow copy\
local headCopyA \= head:copy("NewHead")\
print(headCopyA.Head \== headCube) \--> true\
\
\-- headCopyB contains true copies of head's children as it was passed through a function that recursively copies children\
local headCopyB \= deepCopy(head)\
print(headCopyB.Head \== headCube) \--> false\
\
**@see** [getName](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/ModelPart#getName)\
,, [getChildren](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/ModelPart#getChildren)\
,, [addChild](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/ModelPart#addChild)\
,, [removeChild](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/ModelPart#removeChild)\
,\
\
#### addChild\
\
* * *\
\
Adds the provided ModelPart as one of this ModelPart's children. Beware of adding a parent of this ModelPart as a child! This method returns this ModelPart for method chaining.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `addChild(part ModelPart)` | self ModelPart |\
\
local root \= models.model.root\
local headCopy \= root.Head:copy("NewHead")\
root:addChild(headCopy)\
headCopy:setPos(10,0,0)\
\
**@see** [copy](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/ModelPart#copy)\
,, [setPos](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/ModelPart#setPos)\
,\
\
#### removeChild\
\
* * *\
\
Removes a child from this ModelPart. Takes in the child ModelPart itself. This method returns this ModelPart for method chaining.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `removeChild(partToRemove ModelPart)` | self ModelPart |\
\
local root \= models.model.root\
local head \= root.Head\
root:removeChild(head) \-- Bye bye Head!\
\
\-- Head is still valid and can be re-added later, so long as we keep a variable referencing it.\
print(head) \--> ModelPart(Head)\
\
#### remove\
\
* * *\
\
Removes this ModelPart from the parent's child list. Returns self\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `remove()` | self ModelPart |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
head:remove() \-- Bye bye Head!\
\
\-- Head is still valid and can be re-added, so long as we keep a variable referencing it.\
print(head) \--> ModelPart(Head)\
models.model.root.LeftLeg:addChild(head)\
\
**@see** [addChild](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/ModelPart#addChild)\
,\
\
### Manipulation\
\
Methods relating to manipulating the ModelPart within physical space\
\
#### setPos\
\
* * *\
\
Sets the offset of the the position of the ModelPart. Position translation applies on the local rotation axis.\
\
`nil` values are interpreted as 0.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `setPos(pos [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") )` | self ModelPart |\
| `setPos(x [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) , y [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) , z [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | self ModelPart |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
\
\-- Move 10 units on the local y axis\
head:setPos(0, 10, 0)\
\
#### getPos\
\
* * *\
\
Returns the value that was used for `setPos`. Always 0,0,0 when script begins.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getPos()` | [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
\
print(head:getPos()) \--> vec(0,0,0)\
head:setPos(0, 10, 0)\
print(head:getPos()) \--> vec(0,10,0)\
\
**@see** [setPos](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/ModelPart#setPos)\
,\
\
#### setRot\
\
* * *\
\
Sets the rotation of the ModelPart. Rotates the ModelPart around the PivotPoint.\
\
Angles are interpreted as degrees. `nil` values are interpreted as 0.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `setRot(rot [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") )` | self ModelPart |\
| `setRot(pitch [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) , yaw [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) , roll [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | self ModelPart |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
\
\-- Rotate 45 degrees on the x axis, causing the avatar to look down\
head:setRot(0, 45, 0)\
\
#### getRot\
\
* * *\
\
Returns the value that was used for `setRot`. Will be the Rotation values defined in BlockBench when script begins.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getRot()` | [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
\
print(head:getRot()) \--> vec(0,0,0) -- Most ModelParts will not have a rotation set in blockbench\
head:setRot(45, 0, 0)\
print(head:getRot()) \--> vec(45,0,0)\
\
**@see** [setRot](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/ModelPart#setRot)\
,\
\
#### setScale\
\
* * *\
\
Sets the scale of the ModelPart. Scales the ModelPart around the PivotPoint.\
\
`nil` values are interpreted as 1. If a number is provided for x and both y and z are not defined, x will be used for all 3 axis.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `setScale(scale [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") )` | self ModelPart |\
| `setScale(scaleAll [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | self ModelPart |\
| `setScale(x [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) , y [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) , z [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | self ModelPart |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
\-- Double the size of the head\
head:setScale(2)\
\-- Squishes and stretches the entire model\
models.model:setScale(1.5, 0.75, 1.5)\
\
#### getScale\
\
* * *\
\
Returns the value that was used for `setScale`. Always 1,1,1 when script begins.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getScale()` | [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
\
print(head:getScale()) \--> vec(1,1,1)\
head:setScale(2)\
print(head:getScale()) \--> vec(2,2,2)\
\
**@see** [setScale](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/ModelPart#setScale)\
,\
\
#### setPivot\
\
* * *\
\
Sets the pivot point of the ModelPart. _This overrides the pivot point defined in blockbench._ It is recommended to use [setOffsetPivot](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/ModelPart#setOffsetPivot)\
, instead.\
\
`nil` values are interpreted as 0.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `setPivot(pivot [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") )` | self ModelPart |\
| `setPivot(x [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) , y [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) , z [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | self ModelPart |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
\
\-- For a normal size humanoid model, the Head's pivot point is usually at 0,24,0\
\-- If we assume that the Head cube is an 8x8x8 cube,\
\-- then the head will rotate around the center of the cube instead of the neck\
head:setPivot(0, 28, 0)\
\
#### getPivot\
\
* * *\
\
Returns the Pivot Point defined in BlockBench, or the value set by `setPivot` if it was already overwritten.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getPivot()` | [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
\
\-- The Head group's pivot point for a humanoid model is usually at 0,24,0\
print(head:getPivot()) \--> vec(0,24,0)\
head:setPivot(0,0,0)\
\-- We have completely ruined the rendering of this ModelPart\
print(head:getPivot()) \--> vec(0,0,0)\
\
**@see** [setPivot](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/ModelPart#setPivot)\
,\
\
#### setOffsetRot\
\
* * *\
\
Sets a rotation value that will be added to the ModelPart's rotation.\
\
Angles are interpreted as degrees. `nil` values are interpreted as 0.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `setOffsetRot(rot [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") )` | self ModelPart |\
| `setOffsetRot(pitch [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) , yaw [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) , roll [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | self ModelPart |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
\
\-- ModelParts inherit their rotation from blockbench. The Head usually has a rotation of 0,0,0 for consistency with the vanilla model\
print(head:getRot()) \--> vec(0,0,0)\
\-- Set the offset to 45 degrees on the x axis, causing the avatar to look down\
head:setOffsetRot(0, 45, 0)\
\-- The original rotation is unchanged.\
print(head:getRot()) \--> vec(0,0,0)\
\
\-- setOffsetRot is not additive.\
head:setOffsetRot(0, 25, 0)\
print(head:getOffsetRot()) \--> vec(0,25,0)\
\
**@see** [getRot](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/ModelPart#getRot)\
, [getOffsetRot](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/ModelPart#getOffsetRot)\
,\
\
#### getOffsetRot\
\
* * *\
\
Returns the value that was used for `setOffsetRot`. Will be 0,0,0 when the script begins\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getOffsetRot()` | [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
\
print(head:getOffsetRot()) \--> vec(0,0,0)\
head:setOffsetRot(45, 0, 0)\
print(head:getOffsetRot()) \--> vec(45,0,0)\
\
**@see** [setOffsetRot](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/ModelPart#setOffsetRot)\
,\
\
#### setOffsetScale\
\
* * *\
\
Sets a scale value that will be multiplied with the ModelPart's scale.\
\
`nil` values are interpreted as 1. If a number is provided for x and both y and z are not defined, x will be used for all 3 axis.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `setOffsetScale(scale [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") )` | self ModelPart |\
| `setOffsetScale(scaleAll [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | self ModelPart |\
| `setOffsetScale(x [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) , y [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) , z [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | self ModelPart |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
\-- Double the size of the head\
head:setScale(2)\
\-- Half the size of the head\
head:setOffsetScale(0.5)\
\-- Results in no changes\
\-- I have no idea what this is used for\
\
#### getOffsetScale\
\
* * *\
\
Returns the value that was used for `setOffsetScale`. Always 1,1,1 when script begins.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getOffsetScale()` | [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
\
print(head:getOffsetScale()) \--> vec(1,1,1)\
head:setOffsetScale(2)\
print(head:getOffsetScale()) \--> vec(2,2,2)\
\
**@see** [setOffsetScale](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/ModelPart#setOffsetScale)\
,\
\
#### setOffsetPivot\
\
* * *\
\
Sets a value that will be added to the ModelPart's pivot point.\
\
`nil` values are interpreted as 0.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `setOffsetPivot(pivot [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") )` | self ModelPart |\
| `setOffsetPivot(x [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) , y [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) , z [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | self ModelPart |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
\
\-- If we assume that the Head cube is an 8x8x8 cube and offset the pivot up by 4,\
\-- then the head will rotate around the center of the cube instead of the neck\
head:setOffsetPivot(0, 4, 0)\
\-- Notice that we did not need to know the original pivot point to do this\
\
#### getOffsetPivot\
\
* * *\
\
Returns the value that was used for `setOffsetPivot`. Always 0,0,0 when script begins.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getOffsetPivot()` | [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
\
print(head:getOffsetPivot()) \--> vec(0,0,0)\
head:setOffsetPivot(0,4,0)\
print(head:getOffsetPivot()) \--> vec(0,4,0)\
\
**@see** [setOffsetPivot](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/ModelPart#setOffsetPivot)\
,\
\
#### setMatrix\
\
* * *\
\
Allows you to manually define the matrix used for positioning this ModelPart. Returns self for method chaining.\
\
Using `setPos`, `setRot`, `setScale`, `setPivot`, `setOffsetRot`, `setOffsetScale`, or `setOffsetPivot` will undo `setMatrix`\
\
Using `getPos`, `getRot`, `getScale`, `getPivot`, `getOffsetRot`, `getOffsetScale`, or `getOffsetPivot` will return invalid values while `setMatrix` is in effect.\
\
`getTruePos`, `getTrueRot`, `getTrueScale`, and `getTruePivot` are probably also affected, but nobody tested them yet.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `setMatrix(matrix [Matrix4](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vectors_and_Matrices "Vectors and Matrices") )` | self ModelPart |\
\
\-- no example provided\
\
#### getTruePos\
\
* * *\
\
Returns the position after all calculations are done. This includes `setPos` and the data from all playing Animations.\
\
This does not include ParentTypes or transformations applied from a parent part.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getTruePos()` | [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") |\
\
\-- no example provided\
\
#### getTrueRot\
\
* * *\
\
Returns the rotation after all calculations are done. This includes `setRot`, `setOffsetRot`, and the data from all playing Animations.\
\
This does not include ParentTypes or transformations applied from a parent part.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getTruePos()` | [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") |\
\
\-- no example provided\
\
#### getTrueScale\
\
* * *\
\
Returns the scale after all calculations are done. This includes `setScale`, `setOffsetScale`, and the data from all playing Animations.\
\
This does not include ParentTypes or transformations applied from a parent part.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getTrueScale()` | [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") |\
\
\-- no example provided\
\
#### getTruePivot\
\
* * *\
\
Returns the pivot point after all calculations are done. This includes `setPivot` and `setOffsetPivot`\
\
This does not include ParentTypes or transformations applied from a parent part.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getTruePivot()` | [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") |\
\
\-- no example provided\

### Visual manipulation\
\
Methods relating to modifying how a ModelPart looks\
\
todo: put anything related to renderType, textures, and other visual modifications in here\
\
#### setVisible\
\
* * *\
\
Sets if this ModelPart is visible or not. Children of this ModelPart will also be invisible while this part is invisible.\
\
A value of `nil` is interpreted as `true` on 0.1.4 and below, and `false` on 0.1.5 and above. This message will disappear ~if~ when 0.1.6 is released.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `setVisible(visible [boolean](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | self ModelPart |\
\
local head \= models.model.root.Head\
\
head:setVisible(false) \-- Bye bye Head!\
\
#### getVisible\
\
* * *\
\
Recursively goes up the ModelPart tree until it finds a ModelPart that is invisible, or the ModelPart is `models`\
\
In other words, if a parent part is invisible, this function returns `false`. If all parent parts are visible, this function will return `true` or `nil`. Kinda stupid. This is fixed in 0.1.5 to never return `nil`.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getVisible()` | [bool](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)<br> \| [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)<br> \[_until [0.1.5](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=0.1.5&action=edit&redlink=1 "0.1.5 (page does not exist)")<br>_\] |\
| `getVisible()` | [bool](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)<br> \[_since [0.1.5](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=0.1.5&action=edit&redlink=1 "0.1.5 (page does not exist)")<br>_\] |\
\
local root \= models.model.root.Head\
\
print(root.Head:getVisible()) \--> nil --< this is stupid\
root:setVisible(false) \-- Bye bye root!\
print(root.Head:getVisible()) \--> false\
root:setVisible(true) \-- Welcome back root!\
print(root.Head:getVisible()) \--> true --< aaaaaaaa\
\
#### setColor\
\
* * *\
\
Sets a value to multiply with all pixels on the ModelPart's texture. Children of this ModelPart inherit the color, multiplied with their own.\
\
1,1,1 multiplies all color channels by 1, resulting in the texture unchanged. 0,0,0 results in all channels being black.\
\
Expects values between 0 and 1. Numbers larger than 1 results in undocumented behaviour. `nil` values are interpreted as 1. If only `r` is defined as a number and both `g` and `b` are omitted, `r` is used for all 3 color channels.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `setColor(color [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") )` | self ModelPart |\
| `setColor(colorAll [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | self ModelPart |\
| `setColor(r [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) , g [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) , b [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | self ModelPart |\
\
local root \= models.model.root\
\-- Darken the entire model\
root:setColor(0.5,0.5,0.5)\
\-- Tint the Head red by reducing the other color channels.\
\-- Color is inherited from parents, so the effective color is (0.5, 0.45, 0.45)\
root.Head:setColor(1,0.7,0.7)\
\
\-- If you want to 'reset' a child's color value, extra work is needed.\
\
\-- Color is max red\
local color \= vec(1,0,0)\
local root \= models.model.root\
\-- root has color\
root:setColor(color)\
\-- Through magic and wizardry, this 'resets' the color of Head back to white, dispite it's parent having a non-white color\
root.Head:setColor(\-color + 2)\
\
#### getColor\
\
* * *\
\
Gets the value set by `setColor`. Returns 1,1,1 when script begins.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getColor()` | [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3") |\
\
local root \= models.model.root\
root:setColor(0.5)\
print(root:getColor()) \--> (0.5, 0.5, 0.5)\
root.Head:setColor(1,0.7,0.7)\
// getColor is not recursive\
print(root.Head:getColor()) \--> (1, 0.7, 0.7)\
\
**@see** [setColor](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/ModelPart#setColor)\
,\
\
#### setOpacity\
\
* * *\
\
Sets the opacity of the ModelPart. Children of this ModelPart inherit the opacity, multiplied with their own.\
\
Minecraft has a minimum visible opacity of 0.1. Opacity values lower than 0.1 will not render at all. Needs verification.\
\
Only supported on [RenderTypes](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=RenderType&action=edit&redlink=1 "RenderType (page does not exist)")\
 that support translucency. The default primary RenderType is `TRANSLUCENT`, so most don't have to worry about it.\
\
Expects a value between 0 and 1.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `setOpacity(opacity [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | self ModelPart |\
\
local root \= models.model.root\
\-- Half opacity\
root:setOpacity(0.5)\
\-- Half of half opacity\
root.Head:setColor(0.5)\
\
#### getOpacity\
\
* * *\
\
Gets the value set by `setOpacity`. Returns 1 when script begins.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getOpacity()` | [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) |\
\
local root \= models.model.root\
root:setOpacity(0.5)\
print(root:getOpacity()) \--> 0.5\
root.Head:setOpacity(0.5)\
// getOpacity is not recursive\
print(root.Head:getOpacity()) \--> 0.5\
\
**@see** [setOpacity](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/ModelPart#setOpacity)\
,\
\
#### setLight\
\
* * *\
\
Overrides the lightlevels used to render the ModelPart. Children of this ModelPart inherit the lightlevel.\
\
Expects 2 values between 0 and 15, or `nil`. Providing `nil` will undo the override, allowing Minecraft to control the lightlevel again.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `setLight(light [Vector2](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2 "Vector2")  \| [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | self ModelPart |\
| `setLight(blockLight [integer](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)  \| [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) , skyLight [integer](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)  \| [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | self ModelPart |\
\
local root \= models.model.root\
\-- Max light\
root:setLight(15, 15)\
\
local root \= models.model.root\
\-- set light based on position (This is a fix for broken lighting on World parts)\
function events.tick()\
  local pos \= player:getPos()\
  local blockLight \= world.getBlockLightLevel(pos)\
  local skyLight \= world.getSkyLightLevel(pos)\
  root:setLight(blockLight, skyLight)\
end\
\
**@see** [player:getPos](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=PlayerAPI&action=edit&redlink=1 "PlayerAPI (page does not exist)")\
 [world.getBlockLightLevel](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=WorldAPI&action=edit&redlink=1 "WorldAPI (page does not exist)")\
 [world.getSkyLightLevel](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=WorldAPI&action=edit&redlink=1 "WorldAPI (page does not exist)")\
\
#### getLight\
\
* * *\
\
Gets the value set by `setLight`. Returns `nil` when script begins.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getLight()` | [Vector2](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2 "Vector2") |\
\
local root \= models.model.root\
\
print(root:getLight()) \--> nil\
\
root:setLight(12, 8)\
\
let light \= root:getLight()\
print(light) \--> vec(12, 8)\
print("BlockLightLevel -> ", light.x) \--> "BlockLightLevel -> 12"\
print("SkyLightLevel -> ", light.y) \--> "BlockLightLevel -> 8"\
\
**@see** [setLight](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/ModelPart#setLight)\
,\
\
#### setOverlay\
\
* * *\
\
Overrides the values used for rendering the red damage tint and the white creeper fuse effect. Really only useful for preventing the damage overlay from rendering on stuff like armor.\
\
Valid values for whiteOverlay: 0-15\
\
Valid values for hurtOverlay: 0-7\
\
whiteOverlay is a gradually increasing white tint from 0 - 15\
\
hurtOverlay is an unchanging red tint from 0 - 7.\
\
When set, hurtOverlay overrides whiteOverlay. For whiteOverlay to not be overriden, hurtOverlay needs to be 8 or more.\
\
Providing `nil` will undo the override, allowing Minecraft to control the overlay again.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `setOverlay(overlayVector [Vector2](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2 "Vector2")  \| [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | self ModelPart |\
| `setOverlay(whiteOverlay [integer](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)  \| [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) , hurtOverlay [integer](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) )` | self ModelPart |\
\
local root \= models.model.root\
\-- Damage overlay\
root:setOverlay(0, 0)\
\-- Literally no difference\
root:setOverlay(0, 5)\
root:setOverlay(0, 7)\
\
\-- Doesnt work. Damage overlay overrides white\
root:setOverlay(15, 0)\
\
\-- This works. Max white overlay\
root:setOverlay(15, 15)\
\
\-- This can be used to for preventing the damage overlay on armor\
root:setOverlay(0, 15)\
\
\-- Give control back to Minecraft\
root:setOverlay(nil)\
\
#### getOverlay\
\
* * *\
\
Gets the value set by `setOverlay`. Returns `nil` when script begins.\
\
| Arguments | Return Type |\
| --- | --- |\
| `getOverlay()` | [Vector2](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector2 "Vector2") |\
\
local root \= models.model.root\
\
print(root:getOverlay()) \--> nil\
\
root:setOverlay(8, 15)\
\
let overlay \= root:getOverlay()\
print(overlay) \--> vec(8, 15)\
print("whiteOverlay -> ", overlay.x) \--> "whiteOverlay -> 8"\
print("hurtOverlay -> ", overlay.y) \--> "hurtOverlay -> 15"\
\
**@see** [setOverlay](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/ModelPart#setOverlay)\
,\

# toJson - FiguraMC

| Arguments | Returns |
| --- | --- |
| Table: [table](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) | [string](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1) |

Serializes a table into a JSON string.  
See [parseJson](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/ParseJson "ParseJson")

Navigation
----------

| Documentation |     |     |     |     |     |
| --- | --- |

# Vectors and Matrices - FiguraMC

This page is a [stub](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Stub "wikipedia:Wikipedia:Stub")
. You can help this wiki by [expanding it](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Vectors_and_Matrices&action=edit)

Not to be confused with [Vectors (Global)](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Vectors_(Global)&action=edit&redlink=1 "Vectors (Global) (page does not exist)")
, [Vector](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector "Vector")
, or [Matrices (Global)](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Matrices_(Global)&action=edit&redlink=1 "Matrices (Global) (page does not exist)")
.

Vectors and matrices at their core are **a set of numbers** that represent something (e.g. a Vector3 could represent a position in the world.)

Vectors are one-dimensional; for example, a [Vector3](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Vector3 "Vector3")
 holds 3 numbers. Vectors are most commonly used for representing the position and rotation of things.

Matrices are two-dimensional grids. All matrices are square, so a Matrix3 is a 3 by 3 grid of numbers. Matrices are most commonly used to represent transformations of vectors. For more in-depth information, see [the Wikipedia article on transformation matrices](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Transformation_matrix "wikipedia:Transformation matrix")
.

Vectors
-------

Many functions that take in a vector will also take in the same amount of numbers and internally convert it into a Vector.

Vectors come in 3 types: Vector2, Vector3, and Vector4. The number refers to the size of the vector (Vector4 has 4 numbers, etc.) You can create a vector by using the global method `vec` as shown:

*   vec(x [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
    , y [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
    , z [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
     | [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
    , w [number](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
     | [nil](https://www.lua.org/manual/5.2/manual.html#2.1)
    )

This method will return a vector based on how many arguments you input.

Matrices
--------

Matrices are a set of vectors, which are normally used to change where models are, how they look, etc.

# Abuse filter management - FiguraMC

Welcome to the Abuse Filter management interface. The Abuse Filter is an automated software mechanism of applying automatic heuristics to all actions. This interface shows a list of defined filters, and allows them to be modified.

All filters
-----------

Search optionsExpandCollapse

Deleted filters:

Include deleted filters

Hide deleted filters

Show only deleted filters

Further options:

Hide private filters

Hide disabled filters

Number per page:

2050100250500

Update

| [Filter ID](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Special:AbuseFilter&sort=af_id&limit=50&asc=&desc=1 "Sort descending") | Public description | Consequences | [Status](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Special:AbuseFilter&sort=af_enabled&limit=50 "Special:AbuseFilter") | [Last modified](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Special:AbuseFilter&sort=af_timestamp&limit=50 "Special:AbuseFilter") | [Visibility](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Special:AbuseFilter&sort=af_hidden&limit=50 "Special:AbuseFilter") |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| No results |     |     |     |     |     |

.

any levelsemi protectedfully protectedcentral notice administrator protected

# Unknown

MediaWiki internal error.  
  
Original exception: \[2c81cfb4c579406efca7b1e1\] 2026-02-15 12:39:40: Fatal exception of type "Wikimedia\\Rdbms\\DBConnectionError"  
  
Exception caught inside exception handler.  
  
Set $wgShowExceptionDetails = true; at the bottom of LocalSettings.php to show detailed debugging information.

# Template:Host only - FiguraMC

This API is only available on the host.

For more information, see [Pings](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Pings "Pings")
.

|     |     |     |     |     |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
Template parameters\[[Edit template data](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Template:Host_only&action=edit&templatedata=edit "Template:Host only")\
\]
| Parameter |     | Description | Type | Status |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Kind | `kind` | Noun describing the thing that is host-only<br><br>Suggested values<br><br>`API` `function` `method` `field`<br><br>Default<br><br>API<br><br>Example<br><br>API | Content | optional |
| Additional text | `extra` | Additional content rendered between the heading and the 'for more information' text. | Content | optional |

Retrieved from "[https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Template:Host\_only&oldid=483](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Template:Host_only&oldid=483)

# Template:Notice - FiguraMC

{{{content}}}

|     |     |     |     |     |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
Template parameters\[[Edit template data](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Template:Notice&action=edit&templatedata=edit "Template:Notice")\
\]
This template prefers inline formatting of parameters.
| Parameter |     | Description | Type | Status |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Content | `content` `1` | no description | Content | required |
| Outline | `outline` | Color used for the border, including the left side color swatch.<br><br>Default<br><br>#36c | Unknown | optional |
| Background | `background` | Color used for the background of the box.<br><br>Default<br><br>#def | Unknown | optional |
| Text Color | `textcolor` `color` | Color to use for the box's text<br><br>Default<br><br>#000 | String | optional |
| Outline (Dark mode) | `outline-dark` | Outline color in dark themes. For a quick fix, invert and hue-rotate the light theme by 180deg.<br><br>Default<br><br>#6d9eff | String | optional |
| Background (Dark mode) | `background-dark` | Background color in dark themes.<br><br>Default<br><br>#041424 | String | optional |
| Text color (Dark mode) | `textcolor-dark` | Text color in dark themes.<br><br>Default<br><br>#eee | String | optional |

Retrieved from "[https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Template:Notice&oldid=628](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Template:Notice&oldid=628)

# FiguraMC:Rules - FiguraMC

*   Keep it PG
*   No hateful language
*   Mainspace (no-prefix) pages should be informative content about Figura, community libraries, or addons
*   Example code needs to be tested before publishing!

# Grants - FiguraMC

The following is a list of grants with their associated access to user rights. Users can authorize applications to use their account, but with limited permissions based on the grants the user gave to the application. An application acting on behalf of a user cannot actually use rights that the user does not have however. There may be [additional information](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php?title=Help:Group_rights&action=edit&redlink=1 "Help:Group rights (page does not exist)")
 about individual rights.

| Grant | Rights |
| --- | --- |
| Basic rights `(basic)` | *   Automatically log in with an external user account `(autocreateaccount)`<br>*   Bypass IP blocks, auto-blocks and range blocks `(ipblock-exempt)`<br>*   Edit pages protected as "Allow only autoconfirmed users" `(editsemiprotected)`<br>*   Have one's own edits automatically marked as patrolled `(autopatrol)`<br>*   Not be affected by IP-based rate limits `(autoconfirmed)`<br>*   Not have minor edits to discussion pages trigger the new messages prompt `(nominornewtalk)`<br>*   Read pages `(read)`<br>*   Use of the write API `(writeapi)`<br>*   View a list of unwatched pages `(unwatchedpages)`<br>*   View abuse filters `(abusefilter-view)`<br>*   View detailed abuse log entries `(abusefilter-log-detail)`<br>*   View recent changes patrol marks `(patrolmarks)`<br>*   View the abuse log `(abusefilter-log)` |
| High-volume (bot) access `(highvolume)` | *   Be treated as an automated process `(bot)`<br>*   Mark rolled-back edits as bot edits `(markbotedits)`<br>*   Not be affected by rate limits `(noratelimit)`<br>*   Use higher limits in API queries `(apihighlimits)` |
| Import revisions `(import)` | *   Import pages from a file upload `(importupload)`<br>*   Import pages from other wikis `(import)` |
| Edit existing pages `(editpage)` | *   Add and remove arbitrary [tags](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Special:Tags "Special:Tags")<br>     on individual revisions and log entries `(changetags)`<br>*   Apply [tags](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Special:Tags "Special:Tags")<br>     along with one's changes `(applychangetags)`<br>*   Edit pages `(edit)`<br>*   Edit the content model of a page `(editcontentmodel)`<br>*   Mark edits as minor `(minoredit)` |
| Edit protected pages `(editprotected)` | *   Add and remove arbitrary [tags](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Special:Tags "Special:Tags")<br>     on individual revisions and log entries `(changetags)`<br>*   Apply [tags](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Special:Tags "Special:Tags")<br>     along with one's changes `(applychangetags)`<br>*   Bypass blocked external domains `(abusefilter-bypass-blocked-external-domains)`<br>*   Bypass the spam block list `(sboverride)`<br>*   Edit pages `(edit)`<br>*   Edit pages protected as "Allow only administrators" `(editprotected)`<br>*   Edit the content model of a page `(editcontentmodel)`<br>*   Mark edits as minor `(minoredit)` |
| Edit your user CSS/JSON/JavaScript `(editmycssjs)` | *   Add and remove arbitrary [tags](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Special:Tags "Special:Tags")<br>     on individual revisions and log entries `(changetags)`<br>*   Apply [tags](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Special:Tags "Special:Tags")<br>     along with one's changes `(applychangetags)`<br>*   Edit pages `(edit)`<br>*   Edit the content model of a page `(editcontentmodel)`<br>*   Edit your own user CSS files `(editmyusercss)`<br>*   Edit your own user JSON files `(editmyuserjson)`<br>*   Edit your own user JavaScript files `(editmyuserjs)`<br>*   Mark edits as minor `(minoredit)` |
| Edit your user preferences and JSON configuration `(editmyoptions)` | *   Edit your own preferences `(editmyoptions)`<br>*   Edit your own user JSON files `(editmyuserjson)` |
| Edit the MediaWiki namespace and sitewide/user JSON `(editinterface)` | *   Add and remove arbitrary [tags](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Special:Tags "Special:Tags")<br>     on individual revisions and log entries `(changetags)`<br>*   Apply [tags](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Special:Tags "Special:Tags")<br>     along with one's changes `(applychangetags)`<br>*   Edit other users' JSON files `(edituserjson)`<br>*   Edit pages `(edit)`<br>*   Edit sitewide JSON `(editsitejson)`<br>*   Edit the content model of a page `(editcontentmodel)`<br>*   Edit the user interface `(editinterface)`<br>*   Mark edits as minor `(minoredit)` |
| Edit sitewide and user CSS/JS `(editsiteconfig)` | *   Add and remove arbitrary [tags](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Special:Tags "Special:Tags")<br>     on individual revisions and log entries `(changetags)`<br>*   Apply [tags](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Special:Tags "Special:Tags")<br>     along with one's changes `(applychangetags)`<br>*   Edit other users' CSS files `(editusercss)`<br>*   Edit other users' JSON files `(edituserjson)`<br>*   Edit other users' JavaScript files `(edituserjs)`<br>*   Edit pages `(edit)`<br>*   Edit sitewide CSS `(editsitecss)`<br>*   Edit sitewide JSON `(editsitejson)`<br>*   Edit sitewide JavaScript `(editsitejs)`<br>*   Edit the content model of a page `(editcontentmodel)`<br>*   Edit the user interface `(editinterface)`<br>*   Mark edits as minor `(minoredit)` |
| Create, edit, and move pages `(createeditmovepage)` | *   Add and remove arbitrary [tags](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Special:Tags "Special:Tags")<br>     on individual revisions and log entries `(changetags)`<br>*   Apply [tags](https://wiki.figuramc.org/index.php/Special:Tags "Special:Tags")<br>     along with one's changes `(applychangetags)`<br>*   Create discussion pages `(createtalk)`<br>*   Create pages (which are not discussion pages) `(createpage)`<br>*   Delete single revision redirects `(delete-redirect)`<br>*   Edit pages `(edit)`<br>*   Edit the content model of a page `(editcontentmodel)`<br>*   Mark edits as minor `(minoredit)`<br>*   Move category pages `(move-categorypages)`<br>*   Move pages `(move)`<br>*   Move pages with their subpages `(move-subpages)`<br>*   Move root user pages `(move-rootuserpages)`<br>*   Not create redirects from source pages when moving pages `(suppressredirect)` |
| Upload new files `(uploadfile)` | *   Overwrite existing files uploaded by oneself `(reupload-own)`<br>*   Upload files `(upload)` |
| Upload, replace, and move files `(uploadeditmovefile)` | *   Move files `(movefile)`<br>*   Not create redirects from source pages when moving pages `(suppressredirect)`<br>*   Override files on the shared media repository locally `(reupload-shared)`<br>*   Overwrite existing files `(reupload)`<br>*   Overwrite existing files uploaded by oneself `(reupload-own)`<br>*   Upload files `(upload)`<br>*   Upload files from a URL `(upload_by_url)` |
| Patrol changes to pages `(patrol)` | *   Mark others' edits as patrolled `(patrol)` |
| Rollback changes to pages `(rollback)` | *   Quickly rollback the edits of the last user who edited a particular page `(rollback)` |
| Block and unblock users `(blockusers)` | *   Block or unblock a user from sending email `(blockemail)`<br>*   Block or unblock other users from editing `(block)` |
| View deleted files and pages `(viewdeleted)` | *   Search deleted pages `(browsearchive)`<br>*   View deleted history entries, without their associated text `(deletedhistory)`<br>*   View deleted text and changes between deleted revisions `(deletedtext)` |
| View restricted log entries `(viewrestrictedlogs)` | *   View abuse filters marked as private `(abusefilter-view-private)`<br>*   View hidden abuse log entries `(abusefilter-hidden-log)`<br>*   View log entries of abuse filters marked as private `(abusefilter-log-private)`<br>*   View private logs `(suppressionlog)`<br>*   View the spam block list log `(spamblacklistlog)` |
